zik  n  zik,  tudert-nneɣ  tebna  ɣef  tlelli.  Nekni  d  Imaziɣen  ur 
nessin  azaglu  d  tirni.  Ass-a  ur  nezgir  asif,  ur  nezgir  ilel  a 
nekcem  tamurt  n  medden.  Rruman  d-ikecmen  tamurt-nneɣ  
yezger-d ilel yusa-d ad yerr tamurt-nneɣ ddaw uzaglu. Ur yella 
d  ayen  ara  neqbel.  Anwa  deg-wen  ara  iqeblen  azaglu  n 
Rruman ? 
Imdanen,  tiɣremtin,  timura,  di  ddiq  i  d  tettban  tdukli-nsen. 
Ass-a,  aqlaɣ  neddukel  acku  tesdukel  aɣ  temsalt,  sduklen  aɣ 
iẓuran,  yesdukel-aɣ  uzekka.  Yezmer  uzekka  ad  yili  d  tafat  ma 
neddukel,  yezmer  ad  yili  d  tillas  ma  ur  neddukel.  Timlilit  n 
wass-a  tefka-aɣ-d  tafat  ara  aɣ-yessiwḍen  akin  i  yiɣil,  akin  ɣer 
wussan anda imdanen ur kennun ddaw uzaglu. Tamurt tekker, 
d kenwi i d iɣil-is, d afud-is, d azekka usirem-ines." 
Nebda tikli, abrid-nneɣ ɣer Sirta. 
Si  tedyant  n  Begga,  n  Tala  akk  d  tiɣremtin  nniḍen,  Metellus 
yekcem s lâesker tiɣremtin nniḍen. Di taggara ur riɣ ad yernu 
ad yesserɣ yal tiɣremt n Tmazɣa. Si tedyant-nni n Begga akk d 
Tala,  yal  tiɣremt  seg  ara  zriɣ,  ttiniɣ-asen  yiwen  wawal  :  ma 
yusa d Rruman, ooet tiwwura n tiɣremt llint. Ɣas yekcem ass-a, 
azekka  ad  yeffeɣ,  ad  yafeg  am  tagut  unebdu.  Yif  ad  yekcem 
tiɣremt  ibedden  wala  ad  yesserɣ  ayen  nebna  deg  wacḥal 
iseggassen. 
Akken  i  teffeɣ.  Anida  yewweḍ  Metellus  akk  Marius,  ad  afen 
tiɣremt  llint  tewwura-s.  Netta  iɣil  malen  ɣur-sen  imezdaɣ, 
nekni neooa beddent tiɣremtin-nneɣ, ddren watmaten-nneɣ. 
Tadukli  n  lâesker-nneɣ  akk  d  wid  n  Buxuc,  abrid-is  yiwen. 
Nefra  ɣef  Metellus  ad  as-nekkes  aqerru.  Ur  yella  webrid 
nniḍen. 
Anida  yella  ad  neɣli  fell-as.  Ma  yeffeɣ  si  Tmazɣa,  ad  t-neḍfer 
alamma  d  Utique,  di  tmurt  n  Carthage,  ula  d  tin  d  tamurt-
nneɣ. Nefra, ad d-nuɣal s uqerru-s, anida yebɣa yeffer. 
Deg  webrid  n  Sirta,  nebda  nettheggi  imenɣi  mgal  lâesker  n 
Rruman. Imenɣi yezmer ad yili zdat n Sirta, di Tiddis, neɣ deg 
uzaɣar.  D  Metellus  ad  d-yefken  tasarut-is.  Sirta  nefra  ad  tt-
nekcem, ad nerr tiɣremt i yimawlan-is. Syin tamsalt n Metellus 
ad tefru din neɣ anda nniḍen. 
Mi  yesla  Metellus  s  tdukli-nneɣ,  iga  anezgum  ameqqran. 
Tiḥeôci-nni n Rruman s wayla-s. Metellus yewwet ad aɣ-yebḍu 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
nekk  akk  d  Buxuc.  Tifukal  yessedda  i  Bumelxiô,  yewwet  ad 
tent-yesseddu  i  Buxuc.  Yuzen-d  wid  ad  d-yessiwḍen  awal-is  i 
Buxuc.    Yal  tamacahut  i  yes-s  yewwet  akken  ad  aɣ-yebḍu,  ad 
yeg ugur gar-aneɣ. Di tfukal-is, yenna-yas i Buxuc : "nekni yid-
k ad nemsefam, ur yella ṭṭṛad, ala lxiô i yellan ; ad naru leâqed 
anda  wa  ur  yettaweḍ  wa  ;  tamurt-ik  ur  tt-nkeččem.  Ur ḍeffeô 
Yugurten, di yir abrid i yella ...".  
Buxuc,  yerra-yas  awalen  ilaqen  i  Metellus.  yenna-yas  « ma 
yella  kra  n  leâqed,  netta  d  Yugurten  ara  t-yaru  Metellus,  mi 
yeffeɣ si tlisa n Tmazɣa. Ma d Tamazɣa n Buxuc, Mauretania, 
tebâed akin fell-as ». 
Tadyant  teqqim  akken,  ger  yemnayen d yuzen Metellus  akk d 
wid  d  yuzen  Buxuc  i  Metellus.  Ur  nekcim  Sirta,  ur  nekkis 
aqerruy n Metellus. 
Tusa-d tegrest, yal yiwen yuɣal ɣer wemkan-is, ṭṭṛad ad yekker 
mi ara kksen igefran imeqqranen, ar d-fsin ideflawen.  
Tallit n Marius Caius akk d Sulla 
Yiwen wass yusa-aɣ-d wawal amaynut ; yusa-d si Senat 
n Ruma : Marius yettwafren, yuɣal d netta i d consul (jiniral) 
di  Ruma.  Fran  ad  yas  ɣer  Numidya  deg  wemkan  n  Metellus. 
Imir  Marius  yuɣal  ɣer  Ruma,  yella  din  di  tefrent-nni,  yezger 
nnig lebɣi n Metellus. 
S  isalan  i  d-yusan  si  Ruma  nefhem  s  uzuɣer-nni  i  yezzuɣur 
irennu  Metellus.  Si  tazwara-as,  ziɣ  d  asedhu  kan  i  yaɣ 
yessedhuy. Tamsalt teffeɣ-as afus. 
Nefhem tamuɣli n Ruma : Iôumaniyen ur beddlen tamuɣli-nsen 
ɣef  tmurt-nneɣ.  Anda  ara  d-llin  tiwwura  i  telwit,  ad  d-aznen 
ɣur-i  akken  ad  d  naf  abrid  n  tifrat,  nitni  fernen  Marius,  win 
ara yesseḥmun ṭṭṛad ugar, win ara yernun tardast n tmes akin 
ɣef tlufa n Metellus.  
Marius  ssneɣ-t  di  ṭṭṛad  n  Numance,  d  aâessekriw  deg 
yidammen  nnig  akk  ifesyanen  n  Rruman.  D  argaz  n  wawal, 
iḥemmel  tamurt-is.  Mi  yella  ddaw  Metellus,  ur  as-fsin  i 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
yiɣallen, icudd-it Metellus. Ass-a d netta uɣur d tegra. Fehmeɣ, 
ad as-nuɣal i temsalt seg wadda. 
Di tefsut d yusan  i nesla yezger-d Marius  ɣer Utique, yerna-d 
ibabuôen  n  lâeskeô.  Ass-mi  d  yusa  Marius,  Metellus  tuɣ-it 
yezger  akin,  yuɣal  ɣer  tmurt-is.  Ur  ira  ad  t-id-yaf  Marius,  ur 
ira ad yemlil yid-s di Utique. Gar-asen si tazwara d tismin akk 
d tuzzma. 
Mi d-yewweḍ Marius, yekker, yuɣ abrid n ṭṭṛad.  
Si mi iṣeggem lâesker-is, Marius yesdukel wid yellan akk d wid 
i  d-yerna,    yeffeɣ-d  si  Utique,  yezger-d  tilisa,    yebda  tikli  di 
tmurt n Tmazɣa. 
Amennuɣ  mgal  Metellus  yefka-yaɣ-d  abrid  ara  neḍfeô  di  tallit 
tamaynut mgal Marius. Di tazwara negguni ad yefreq lâesker-
is. Neooa-ten kecmen-d tamazɣa, teddun iberdan-nsen, beḍḍun 
ɣef  teɣremtin.  Simmal  ferqen,  simmal  tazmert-nsen  tferreq 
ugar.  Yal  tiɣremt    wwḍen  ad  afen  tiwwura  llint.  Ur  yella 
imenɣi, ur tella tmes, ur  lluẓen imezdaɣ-nni, ur rɣant tzeɣwa.  
Nufa abrid-nni yelha. 
Nekk akk d Buxuc, negguni ass-is deg ara nedwi fell-asen. 
Acḥal n tikkelt i neɣli ɣef lâesker n Rruman anda ur aɣ-ggunin. 
Snat  tyitwin kan, mi ten-nesduqqes, neqqed kra seg-sen,  ad d 
neffeɣ  seg  wennar.  Nitni  ad  ɣillen  nerwel,  nugad-iten,  nekni  
ad  neddu  deg  webrid-nneɣ  ad  nesduqqes  tarbaât  nniḍen. 
Akken i asen-nedda acḥal n wagguren. D axbacen kan, imenɣi 
ameqqran ur d-yella. Marius nessen-it yeḥrec, nekni nunef seg 
webrid-is. 
Tiyita tameqqrant tamezwarut n Marius tusa-aɣ-d si tiɣremt n 
Gafsa. 
D  tikkelt  tamezwarut  i  yedda  lâesker  n  Rruman  deg  webrid 
aɣezfan,  igzem  azaɣar  nekni  ur  nesla.  Nuɣ  tannumi,  di  yal 
tikkelt ara mbiwlen lâeskeô-nsen, nekni ad aɣ-d-yaweḍ wawal. 
Di  yal  tiɣremt,  di  yal  tiɣilt,  di  yal  taqiccuôt,  nesbedd  wid 
yeggunin, wid iẓeôôen iberdan uɣen Iôumaniyen.  Anda ddan, 
nekni  nesla.  Tiyita  n  Gafsa  tenser-aɣ.  Marius  mi  yeffeɣ  s 
lâesker-is, yezzi deg webrid, yunef akka d wakka. Mi yewweḍ 
asif  n  Tanius,  ibeddel  abrid.  Ihegga  tiyelwin  i  waman,  syin 
yeffeɣ  seg  webrid  ameqqran.  Iteddu  deg  yiḍ,  iteffer  deg  wzal. 
Ur iẓri yiwen anida i yella. 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
Yiwet yiwet armi wwḍen tawwurt n tiɣremt n Gafsa. 
Mi yewweḍ Gafsa, iɣli ɣef imezdaɣ n dinna ur bnan ɣef yiman-
nsen. Marius yurar urar-nni n Metellus ass-mi yekcem Begga. 
Mi qrib ad yaweḍ, yezwer imnayen Imaziɣen, wid yellan ddaw 
ufus n Gawda. Mi ten-id-ẓran at Gafsa nwan d at tmurt s tidet. 
Taggara,  mi  teddun  ad  kecmen,  at  Gafsa  ẓran-d  ɣer  deffir 
lâeskeô n Rruman. Yekker herwel. 
Akken ad yessekcem tawekka di tmurt-nneɣ, akken ad yeg iɣisi 
ur nselleɣ, Marius yeseḥôec Gawda, gma-nni, yerra-t d acengu 
n Tmazɣa. Marius yefka-as lâeskeô, iteddu deg umennuɣ  mgal 
at tmurt-is. Iôeggem-as Marius ad yuɣal d agellid ma yemmut 
Yugurten.    Si  tedyant-nni,  deg  wennar  imenɣi,  tikwal  d  at 
tmurt-iw  i  d  ixûimen.  Sya  d  syin,  d  irgazen  Imaziɣen  i 
yettnaɣen, d idim Amaziɣ i yemmaren. 
At  Gafsa-nni,  lemmer  gan  am  akken  i  asen-nenna,  ad  llin 
tiwwura  n  teɣremt,  nitni  beddlen  tikli.  Mi  d  ẓran  imnayen  n 
Rruman,  yekker  yimenɣi  mgal  yemnayen-nni  ikecmen  syin 
medlen tiwwura, bedden i tyita mgal wid d iteddun. 
Taggara,  teffeɣ  akken  teffeɣ.  At  Gafsa  ur  zmiren  ad  qablen 
ahdum  n  lâesker  i  yasen-yezzin.  Tiremt  kan,  Iôumaniyen 
hudden ifergan i as-yezzin, kecmen tiɣremt s ujenwi deg ufus. 
Wid  meqqren  nɣan-ten  din,  wiyaḍ  wwin-ten-id  d  aklan.  
Tiɣremt  n  telwit  n  tezdayin  n  tini,  tuɣal-as  d  yir  targit,  ijdi 
amellal yuɣal d azeggaɣ seg yidammen. 
Tiyita-nni  n  Gafsa  tekkes-as  akukru  i  Marius.  Tamurt  yessen-
itt, irgazen llan, yenwa teswa-as-d s wedfel. 
Acemma  kan  deffir  tadyant  n  Gafsa,    Marius  igzem  Tamazɣa  
seg yixef ɣer yixef, ikcem akal yellan tama n wasif n Melwen, 
talast  gar  Nekni  akk  d  tmurt  n  Buxuc.    Din,  iqsed  ad  ikcem 
Tawrirt. 
Tawrirt  tebna  ɣef  weẓru  ameqran,  di  tlemmast  uzaɣar.  Yal 
tama  d  acôuf  ur  yezmir  ad  yali  wemdan,  ur  yezmir  yiddew. 
Abrid-is  seg  yiwet  tama  kan  i  yella,  injer  s  ufus  deg  weẓru, 
yeḍyeq,  yesuddem ; win imalen deg-s ad yezg deg yiceôfan n 
wadda.  Ifellaḥen,  s  yiwen  i  sezriyen  izgaren,  tistan  neɣ 
igemren-nsen.  Amur  ameqqran  bennun-asen  ifergan  deg 
uzaɣar. 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
Tawrirt d tiɣremt yeddurin am lâec igider. Tama ufella, d awrir 
zun yenjer-it ufus. Di tlemmast n luḍa-nni tɣez tala.  Imezdaɣ-
is  si  zik  n  zik  ur  yezmir  yiwen  ad  asen-yekcem  tasga.  Sin 
yergazen  zemren  ad  gen  afrag  ɣef  tewwurt  s  ineccaben-nsen. 
Ifellaḥen,  yal  ass  ad  adren  akessar,  ad  xedmen  tibḥirin  neɣ 
igran-nsen, mi yeɣli yiṭij ad alin ɣer tkanna-nsen di Tewrirt. 
Am Metellus di Begga, Am ass-a  Marius di  Tewrirt, yenwa ad 
aɣ-d-yaf dinna, nekk akk d Buxuc, ad yaf agerruj n Tmazɣa, ad 
aɣ-d-yeṭṭef  s  ufus.  Marius  yezzi  i  Tewrirt,  syin  yessedhem 
lâesker-is ɣer ifergan. Yekker yimenɣi. Win deg-sen iqerben ad 
d-yečč  tiyita,  ad  yemmet  neɣ  ad  d-yerwel  ɣer  deffir.  Wid 
yessulin  tigejda  i  walluy,  mazal  ttawḍen  ɣer  yixef  mi  ara  ten-
id-yečč  ujajiḥ  n  tmes  neɣ  n  weẓru,  ad  grirben  ɣer  deffir.    Yal 
adham ad yawi ɣer lmut  tissi n lâesker n Marius. 
At  Tewrirt  ur  as-gan  aɣilif.  Afrag  yella,  aman  d  wučči  llan, 
irgazen llan. Yal tikkelt ad grirben Iôumaniyen akessar ad ten-
id-ḍefrent  teɣratin  n  tlawin.  Marius  yeffeɣ-it  leâqel.  Akken 
yexdem ur as-yufa tawwurt. 
yefra-tt  d  yiman-is,  iteddu  ad  yekkes  lâesker-nni  i  yezzin  i 
Tewrirt,  ad  yuɣal  akin  ɣer  tmurt  ufella,  mi  as-yekcem  ɣer 
uqiḍun-is  yiwen  uâsekriw  ,  n  tmurt  Liguria31,  yenna-as  i 
Marius : 
-  "Ufiɣ  abrid  yessufuɣen  ɣer  tiɣilt  n  Tewrirt.  Lliɣ  leqḍeɣ 
iâôusen, uliɣ acôuf si tama nniḍen, deffir, armi ufiɣ yiwet tasaft 
temɣi-d  ɣef  weslaḍ.  Uliɣ  ɣef  tasaft-nni,  ddiɣ  ɣef  ufurk-nni 
yerran  d  asawen  armi  d-ufiɣ  iman-iw  ɣef  tqacuct,  di  Tewrirt 
ufella  ;  ẓriɣ  s  wallen-iw  Imaziɣen  yellan  din,  nitni  ur  iyi-d-
ẓran,  sentleɣ  iman-iw.  Syin  uɣaleɣ  d  ansi  kkiɣ.  Ma  tebɣiḍ  ad 
uɣaleɣ akk d wiyaḍ ad sen-mmleɣ abrid !". 
Marius  terkeb-it  tawla.  Iqdef  aâsekriw-nni,  yefka-yas  wid  ɣef 
yettkel, ddan yid-s. Qbel ad alin, kksen taselsa n Rruman, kksen 
uzzal,  lsan  am  Imaziɣen,    ulin  seg  webrid-nni  n  yeârusen, 
wwḍen  taqacuct-nni  n  Tewrirt.  Mi  d  uɣalen,  d  awal  d-yenna 
umezwaru-nni  i  d-nnan  ineggura-nni.  Abrid  yella.  Marius 
yeffreḥ. Yufa telli-yas-d tewwurt anda ur yessarem.

imukan  n 
tyita  n  zdat  nebla 
Azekka-nni  kan  ihegga  tarbaât,  yerna-asen  lbuq  akken  mi 
wwḍen  luḍa  ufella  n  Tewrirt  ad  wwten  lbuq.  yessels-asen 
iceṭṭiḍen  n  Imaziɣen  akken  ad  fken  anza  ɣer  Imaziɣen  n 
tewrirt.  Akken  i  teffeɣ.  Azekka-nni,  mi  yulin  wa  deffir  wa,  s 
leḥder,  taggara  kecmen  luḍa  ufella.  Mi  wwḍen  akken  llan, 
dduklen  ɣer  yiwen  wemkan,  heggan  iman-nsen  syin  bdan 
tiyita n lbuq, tilawin yeddurin ɣer deffir suɣent, dɣa at Tewrirt 
yeffeɣ-iten  laâqel,  acengu  yekka-asen-d  si  deffir.  Mi  d  bernen

irgazen. 
Iôumaniyen, nitni sseḥman-d tiyita s wadda, ulin-d seg igudar, 
kecmen-d  talemmast  n  weɣrem.    Syin,  win  ara  yemten  yella, 
win a yenɣen ulac. Imenɣi yefra. Wid ufan dinna d imedduren 
nɣan-ten,  ur  d  yegri  yiwen,  d  aqcic,  d  argaz  neɣ  d  tameṭṭut. 
Gan timecreḍt deg at Tewrirt. Snegren-ten. 
Deffir tedyant-nni n Tewrirt i d-yusa Sulla si Ruma, yewweḍ-d 
ɣer tmurt, yerna-d lâesker i yimenɣi.  Senat n Ruma yelli-asen 
tawwurt. Marius akk d Sulla gan ayen i umi zemren. Abrid n 
ṭṭṛad yenjeô zun d iɣzer.  
Si  tisin-nni  n  Marius  d  Sulla,  kkseɣ  asirem.  Ur  yella  wayen 
gguniɣ  si  tama  n  Rruman.  Abrid-nsen  d  ṭṭṛad,  abrid-nneɣ  d 
ṭṭṛad. Tama ad tekk di tayeḍ.  
Asirem  n  talwit  yekkes,  zziɣ-d  tikkelt  nniḍen  i  tmura.  Awal  i 
asen-nniɣ yiwen : 
- "Ay atmaten ! Aôumani yekcem-d tamurt, Aôumani ilaq-as ad 
yeffeɣ tamurt. D  nitni i d-izegren ilel Agrakal,  mačči d nekni. 
Yiwet tmurt kan i nla. Ur nezmir ad tt-neoo, neɣ ad tt-nefk  d 
tarzeft i Uôumani. Yiwen webrid i yellan ass-a, d abrid n yiseɣ, 
d  abrid  n  tnekra,  ad  nesenger  ajôad  d-ikecmen.  Anida  tufam 
lâesker n Marius, ur din awexxer, ur din inif. Win d-yessutren 
leânaya  eoo-it,  ma  d  wayeḍ  zwi-t  !  Iôumaniyen  i  d-yusan  ad 
sen-neddukel  am  zun  d  aweṭṭuf.  Ma  s  tubbya  kan  nezmer  ad 
ten-nessenger.  Ay  atmaten !  Ma  teddukel  tcemlit-nneɣ,  ad 
nesergagi  Ruma.  Ass-a  nwen,  azekka  nwen,  tamurt  d  kenwi  i 
tegguni !" 
Mi  d-zziɣ  i  tmurt,  ufiɣ  yuki-d  ugar  uẓar-nni  n  tnekra,  uɣeɣ 
abrid ɣer tmurt n Buxuc. 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
Si  tedyant-nni  mi  nedda  ad  nekcem  Sirta,  teqqim  akken  gar-
aneɣ. Uɣaleɣ ɣur-s akken ad nessemɣer admer ara yessergagin 
Rruman. 
Mi ufiɣ Buxuc, fkiɣ-as tamuɣli-w amek ilaq ad as-neddu i ṭṭṛad 
mgal Rruman. Tamurt yiwet akal yiwen, laûel-nneɣ yiwen, iles 
yiwen.  Nniɣ-as ilaq-aɣ ad nekkes talast yellan gar-aneɣ si tallit 
n  Sifaks,  si  tallit  n  Masensen.  Talast  ibeḍḍun  ad  tt-nekkes,  ad 
nerr  tin  yesduklen,  anda  yebɣa  nekk  qebleɣ.  Nniɣ-as,  Sifaks  d 
jedd-nneɣ,  Masensen  d  jedd-nneɣ.  Ma  nesdukel  iɣallen-nneɣ 
ad  nerr  leqder  i  tmurt-nneɣ.  Ad  nekkes  imennuɣen  gar-aneɣ, 
ad nekkes ayen i aɣ-yebḍan ad nesemɣer ayen i aɣ-yesduklen. 
Nniɣ-as  ad  aɣ-zzmen  wid  ara  d-yekkren  azekka  ma  ur  nuɣ 
abrid  n  tdukli.  Ad  aɣ-yezzem  wakal  ɣef  nteddu  ma  nuɣ  yir 
abrid ass-a. Abrid-nneɣ ass-a d abrid n yiseɣ, d abrid n tissas. 
Tikemmict  n  Rruman  i  d  yusan,  ma  neddukel,  ad  tt-nesselfeɣ 
am  tkemmict-nni  n  tizwal.  Aôumani  d-ikecmen  ass-a  tama 
ufella,  ma  yessers  iḍaôôen-is,  azekka  ad  yekcem  tama  wadda. 
Aôumani ur yessin ala awal n yiɣil, ala awal n tummeẓt akk d 
wezduz.  Aôumani  yusa-d  ɣef  tkeckult  n  wesɣar  idegger-itt-id 
waḍu  deg  yilel,  azekka  ad  yuɣal  ansi  i  d-yekka,  ad  t-idegger 
waḍu n tnekra-nneɣ, abrid-is akin ɣer Ruma. 
Buxuc ifka-yi-d tameẓẓuɣt, yuɣ abrid n jedd-is. 
Nesdukkel  lâesker-nneɣ,  nuɣ  abrid  ɣer  tmurt  anda  yella 
Marius. 
Wid  nesbedd  deg  yiberdan,  deg  yicuqar,    ayen  yellan  ɣef  tiṭ-
nsen. Anda mbawlen Iôumaniyen, ad aɣ-d-yaweḍ wawal. 
Mi  nella  nteddu  deg  webrid  i  d-nemlal  amnay  s  wegmer-is 
iteddu-d  s  tazzla.    Isalan  i  yaɣ-d-yewwi  sfeôḥen-aɣ  :  "Marius 
akk  d  lâesker-is  llan  teddun  di  tzaɣart  yellan  akin  zdat,  deffir  
yiɣil". 
Niqal ad neddu acḥal n wagguren ara ntezzi si tmurt ɣer tmurt 
akken  ad  d-naf  lateô  n  Marius,  taggara  yeɣli-d  netta  deg 
webrid-nneɣ. 
Din,  nbeddel  tikli,  nefka  imnayen  zwaren  ɣer  zdat  ad  aɣ-d- 
awin  isalan  n  wanda  llan,  acḥal  i  yellan,  anwa  abrid  deg 
teddun.  Nekk  d  Buxuc  nesemlal-d  ifesyanen-nneɣ  ad  nheggi 
tiyita.  Nteddu, nferru-tent amek ara as-neddu i yimenɣi mgal 
Marius.

Yebda iɣelli wass mi nemlal Marius d lâeskeô-is deg yelmaten. 
Tamurt nekni nessen-itt, d azal neɣ d iḍ, irgazen-nneɣ zemren 
ad nnaɣen akken ran. Nebla ma nezzi nefka tissi tamezwarut n 
yemnayen  teɣli fella-asen  am  tmedda. Qbel ad rren tiyita, mi 
llan  tezzin  akken  ad  gen  afrag  yezzin,  nekni  nerna  tissitin  n 
yergazen nniḍen. Yekker uhetwir, nekni nekkat, nitni kkaten. 
Tiṭ-nneɣ nekni ad asen-nezzi, ad sen-neg tasraft anda yiwen ur  
d-iteffeɣ.  Nek  sya,  Buxuc  syin,  tekker  tɣebbart,  simmal 
nessiḍyiq annar, simmal nẓeô nferrez anda nekkat. S terbaât n 
yemnayen  yellan  yid-i,    kecmeɣ  di  tlemmast  akken  ad  awḍeɣ 
Marius,  nekni  nekkat,  nitni  ḥebbken  akken  ad  snesren  iman-
nsen. Ajenwi yedda, timseggeft tedda, aneccab yedda. Yal tama 
tekkat, tettazzal, tnehhet, nettuɣu, tekker tɣebbaôt, irgazen wa 
ibedd  ɣef  iḍarren-is,  wa  yesred  am  uceṭṭiḍ.    Yal  tikkelt  mi 
wwteɣ  ad  qerbeɣ  anda  nwiɣ  yella  Marius,    taggara  tiyita, 
adham  n  yemnayen  ad  aɣ-d-rren  ɣer  deffir,  ad  aɣ-sinfen  ɣer 
yeffus neɣ zelmeḍ. 
Imenɣi yeḥma, iṭij yebda iɣelli, irgazen-nneɣ am izmawen. 
Acemma  kan  tenɣes  tyita,  Iôumaniyen  bdan  nesren  d  tidist. 
Agus-nni i asen-nhegga ur yeṭṭif, Marius akk d kra n lâesker-is 
nesren,  syin  uɣen  amkan  deg  yiwen  wegni,  yufrar-d  asawen. 
Ger  iôumaniyen-nni,  win  snesren  iḍaôôen-is  yenser,  wayeḍ 
yečča-t uneccab neɣ ajenwi. 
Lâeskeô  n  Rruman,  ɣas  ẓran  mačči  ɣef  tmurt-nsen  i  kkaten, 
mačči  d  akal-nsen  i  ɣef  ttnaɣen,  nitni  ssnen-as  i  yimenɣi. 
Tussna imenɣi lemden-tt, rnan ttaɣen awal ugar. Akken i asen-
yenna  ufesyan  ad  aɣen  abrid-is.  Marius  yezwar-asen  ɣer 
wegni-nni,  nitni  ddan  di  later-is,  teddun  kkaten-d  ɣer  deffir,  
nekni nedda deg yiḍaôôen-nsen. Iḍ yeɣli-d, imenɣi yefra. 
Nefra abrid-is nekk akk d Buxuc.  Skud tella taffza, nezzi-as-d s 
lâesker  i wegni zun d taxatemt.  Ur  tella tardast nezgel,  yiwen 
uâsekriw n Rruman ur yezmir ad yeffeɣ syin, awtul ur yezmir 
ad yenser. 
Nemsefham  nekk  d  Buxuc  i  tyita  mi  ara  ad  yali  wass.    Ansi 
wenten ad d ffɣen Iôumaniyen, nekni ad ten-nesni d asnay.  Mi 
nemsefraq,  yal  wa  yerra  anda  llan  lâesker-is.    Neẓra  ad  yiɣzif 
yiḍ.

Akken  sersen  iman-nsen  Imaziɣen-nneɣ,  ssaɣen  iḥeoouoa  n 
tmes,  dɣa kkren i wbendir d lɣiḍa. Tarewla-nni yerwel lâesker 
n Rruman yeffer, ɣillen dayen yefra imenɣi. Abendir yeḥma seg 
tyita,  mačči  d  ayen  ara  tessusmeḍ.    Atmaten-nneɣ  smeɣren 
adriz, afus yekkat, tiqesôit tekkat tadersit.  Mi nella nesseḥmay 
adriz, nnig-nneɣ Marius akk d lâesker-is xemten, ur yella ûûut, 
ur yella wawal, ssusmen am zun mmuten. 
Mi  yedda  yiḍ,  Imaziɣen-nneɣ  feclen,  ssusmen,  win  yeâyan  ad 
isers  iman-is  ad  igen  gar  watmaten-is,  armi  d-ters  tsusmi. 
Gran-d iâessasen bedden akin. 
Lawan-nni kan deg âziz yiḍes, atmaten-nneɣ ẓlen, imir i yesker 
aɣebbar Marius akk d lâesker-is. Di tlemmast n yiḍ i d-heggan 
iman-nsen  ad  nesren.  Uɣen-d  takessart  d  adham,  s  tazzla  d 
usuɣu,  lbuq  yekkat,  ajenwi  yekkat,  aneccab  yekkat.  Mazal  d 
nseggem  iman-nneɣ  i  tyita,  nitni  zrin  akin,  nesren  i  tcebbakt- 
nni i asen-nga. Win nɣan nɣan-t, win rekḍen rekḍen-t. Marius 
yenser i lmut. 
Sduqsen-aɣ  asduqqes-nni  yelhan.  Anda  ilaq  d  nekni  ara  ten- 
yesduqqsen  acemma  kan  qbel  ad  yali  wass,  Marius  yugar-aɣ 
tiḥerci, yezwar talalit n wass. 
Timlilit  n  Yelmaten  tefka-aɣ-d  udem  n  yimenɣi.  Marius  i  d 
neṭṭef gar ifassen-nneɣ, inser-aɣ s tmussni-s, s tiḥḥerci n ṭṭṛad. 
Ger  wid  ukud  nennuɣ,  icban  Bestia,  Albinus  neɣ  Metelllus,  
ɣur-i  Marius  yerna  adar  s  tmussni  n  ṭṭṛad.  Ma  zik  imenɣi  d 
adrar, ass-a d igenni. Akken i as-nekka i tedyant-nni nekk akk 
d Buxuc ur as-nufa ixef-is. Amek i nettwakellex akken ? Amek 
i aɣ-tenser ?  Nečča-tt teḥma. 
Ur  tella  din  teɣzef  n  wawal.    Akken  i  aɣ-yekkes  uzaylal-nni, 
nserreo, nedda deffir Marius d lâesker-is. 
Marius iteddu, nekni nedda di lateô-is. Uḍan ussan nteddu deg 
webrid-is. Abrid n Marius iteddu ɣer Sirta. Ass wis ôebâa neɣli 
fella-asen. 
Mi  teddun  deg  webrid-nsen,  sersen  ad  sgunfun  ad  segmen 
iman-nsen,  nekni    nfuôes  tagnit,  nezzi-asen.  Annar  imenɣi 
ihegga. 
Nekcem  annar,  nekk  sya,  Buxuc  syin,  newwet  ad  nesnefsusi 
agus-nni-nsen.  Di  tazwara  fkiɣ  imnayen  ɣer  zdat,  d  nitni  i  d 
azduz  amezwaru  n  tyita  ;  yugar  i  srewten  igemren  i  wwten

yergazen  s  ineccaben  neɣ  s  ijenwiyen.  Iôumaniyen  zzin, 
swezlen annar akken ad miqraben. Marius akk d Sulla llan di

yessefcel s tuzzya-nni i asen-nezzi. 
Acemma kan mi teḥma tyita armi neẓra yewweḍ-d s lâesker-is

Bilak32,  mmi-s  n  Buxuc.  Mi  d-yewweḍ  kan

sersen, ur sgunfan, kecmen  annar imenɣi. 
Imenɣi-nni yal tikkelt yettbeddil udem, Buxuc netta d imnayen-

tama yeṭṭef. Seg wakken teḥma, taggara ur yeẓra yiwen anwa i 
d  axsim-is.  Wa  yekkat,  wa  yesdari,  wa  yuzzel,  wa  yesred,  wa 
yemmut. Ma teɣli-d tmellalt seg igenni ur d tettaweḍ ɣer tmurt.  
Tameddit n wass, mi d-yeɣli yiḍ yal yiwen yejbed lâesker-is ɣer 
deffir. Azekka-nni, nuɣal ɣer imenɣi am yiḍelli-nni. Si mi tebda 
tyita, Buxus yejbed lâesker akin ɣer deffir. 
Mi  yefra  imenɣi,  tama  ur  tekka  di  tayeḍ.  Marius  akk  d  Sulla 
sduklen irgazen-nsen akin, nekni nezzi-d ɣer deffir, nessenser-
d widen ijerḥen. Irgazen feclen deffir imenɣi amezwaru, tikli n 
tlata  wussan  d  aḥbak,  rnu-yas  imenɣi  n  wass-a.  Tazmert  s 
talast-is.  Annar-nni  neooa  ur  yelli  d  win  ara  ẓrent  wallen. 
Irgazen,  igemren,  wa  yemmut  wa  iteddu  ɣer  lmut,  wa  yenta 
deg-s uneccab deg yidis inehhet, wa icelleḥ s ujenwi yekkat ad

uhicuô.  Agni  yuɣal  d  azeggaɣ  s  yidim.  Ur  tella  d  tamuɣli  n 
tudert.  Ger  wid  yemmuten  d  wid  iteddun  ɣer  lmut,  llan

imeqqranen,

Marius  ikemmel  abrid-is  akin,  deg  webrid  n  Sirta,    Buxuc33 
yesdukel lâesker-is, yeṭṭef yiwet tiɣilt akin, nekni neqqim din ad 
nenṭel irgazen-nneɣ.  Neqqim ad as-nesefru i tedyant yeḍran. 
Tagrest  tusa-d,  Marius  yuli  akin  ɣer  tama  n  Carthage,  yerna 
yesdukel lâesker-is di teɣremtin ṭṭfen di Tmazɣa, yecban Sirta, 
Zama. Buxuc yuɣal ɣer wexxam-is, nekk uɣaleɣ i tazzla akken 
ad  d-snekreɣ  tamurt  d  amaynut  i  Marius.  Ma  yella  ccek, 
aneggaru-yagi  yesban-d  anda  i  tent-nuɣ.  Nuɣ-itent  di  tuddsa. 
Yal  tikkelt,  deg  wennar,  mi  yekker  yimenɣi,  atmaten-nneɣ  ad 
dwin  akka  d  wakka,  zun  ɣer  tesḍaḍ  n  wewtul  neɣ  n  yilfan. 
Adway-nni  ur  yella  d  abrid.  Ilaq-aɣ  ad  nernu  aselmed  ugar  i 
lâesker-nneɣ.  Di  tuddsa  kan  i  aɣ-ifen  Rruman,  nekni  ad  as-
neqqim. 
Imenɣi  ɣezzif,  walaɣ  iteddu  ad  yiɣzif  ugar,  nekni  ilaq-aɣ  ad 
nesdari  ilmeẓyen-nneɣ.  Mačči  d  ahmal  kan  s  yedmaren  ɣer 
zdat.  Imenɣi  s  webrid-is,  s  tuddsa-s,  am  tiddas-nni  n  yelqafen 
netturar ɣef teblaḍin. Yal alqaf yeddukel akk d wid yezwaren, 
yerna  ihegga  tiyita  i  yelqafen  d-iteddun.  Tuddsa  Teḍres, 
temcuddal. 
Imenɣi mgal Rruman friɣ-tt, ad as-nbeddel abrid. 
Ilaq-aɣ ad as-neqqim skud ur  nhegga  lâesker am  akken  i  ten-
ihegga Rruman. Tiyita n Yelmaten, tin n Sirta fkant-aɣ-d talast 
yellan gar-aɣ d Rruman. Tidet, ɣas ṭṭfen tiɣremtin, zzin agadir 
d afrag, tamurt d nekni i tt-yeṭṭfen. Ɣas ad nanef i yimenɣiyen 
imeqqranen,  ansi  kkan  ad  aɣ-d-afen  zdat-nsen,  yal  takemmict 
n lâesker-nsen i d-yeffɣen si teɣremt  ad tenger, anida kkan ad 
afen  tasraft  deg  webrid-nsen.  Ad  asen-neddu  s  tyita  n  tuqqsa, 
am tuqqsa n waôeẓ. 
Akka  i  as-ddiɣ.  Mi  nefra  nekk  akk  d  yifesyanen-nneɣ,  yal 
tarbaât tuɣ abrid-is. I yal tiɣmert n tmurt  ad nessiweḍ awal, ad 
nessiweḍ asirem i tnekra yugaren tin yezrin.

Di  tallit-nni  deg  lliɣ  tedduɣ  deg  yiberdan,  ôwiɣ  akessar  d

yid-sen.  Ayen  i  umi  zemreɣ  giɣ-t.  Ulac  abrid  i  asen-d-kkiɣ

Makawsen,  tiṭ  n  Rruman  d  anekcum  ɣer  Tmazɣa  s  yiɣil-nsen.  
Ayen d-yernan ɣer zdat d tisebbiwin kan. 
Mi sliɣ Buxuc yefka irgazen ɣer Sirta, akken ad ẓren Marius, di

Urfan  d  urfan,  tikwal  llan,  tikwal  zrin.  Taggara,  ufiɣ  tikli  n 
Buxuc  tezmer  ad  tili  ur  tezlig.  Marius  di  Sirta  i  yella,  ɣer  din 
kan ara yazen Buxuc irgazen-is. 
Di  tallit  n  yimenɣi,  Buxuc  yusa-d  netta  d  mm-is,  wwin-d 
lâesker  nnig  wayen  ssarmeɣ.  Kecmen  annar  imenɣi,  wwten 
ayen i umi zemren. Acḥal n yergazen i aɣ-yemmuten. Taggara 
ɣas tiyita-nni zdat Sirta ur aɣ-teffiɣ, nitni fkan-d tazmert-nsen. 
Ass-a ma Buxuc yenwa abrid yessuffuɣen d awal d Marius,  ar 
d-yemɣi ad iban ! 
Seg yiwet tama, awal yelha. Di lawan-nni n wawal, imenɣiyen 
imeqqranen  ad  neɣsen.  Anda  yella  usirem,  ineqqes  weḥḍam 
imenɣi.  Nekni,  di  lawan-a  ad  nesker  lâesker  yecban  Rruman. 
Ayen i ɣezzif wawal yelha. 
Ass-mi  ẓriɣ  Buxuc,  nniɣ-as  ad  iyi-d-yefk  amek  yessedda  awal 
netta d Marius, Sulla neɣ wiyaḍ. Awal-is yegzem : "zik d kečč 
kan i iqublen Rruman, ass-a nella ɣer tama-k nesaweḍ tanekra-
nneɣ  ɣer  webrid  imenɣi.  Iôumaniyen,  ẓran  anda  maleɣ,  ẓran 
tazmert-nneɣ ma neddukel. Yella wawal ɣur-neɣ, neqqar « ma 
tseɣleḍ  wwet  ;  ma  ur  tezmireḍ  ur  sɣal »  ,  nekni  nekker-d, 
newwet.  Ass-a  ma  neqqim  i  wawal  ur  tella  deg-s  tuzzma.  Ihi 
nekk walaɣ, Rruman yif-it ad yili si tama-nneɣ, wala ad yili d 
acengu-nneɣ.  Ma zemreɣ ad ssinfeɣ tallit-a deg nella ɣer tifrat, 
anida yella wugur ?"

Ayen  riɣ  ad  as-skecmeɣ  i  Buxuc  ɣer  wallaɣ-is :  d  tikerkas,

Ayen nniḍen akk d urar, d tuzya n wawal. Takti yagi tekcem-

Atmaten-nneɣ  i  yellan  di  tmurt  n  Carthage,  di  Utique, 
ṣṣawḍen-aɣ-d  awal.    Marius  simmal  yessekcam-d  lâesker 
irennu-d, si Ruma.  Win yessarmen talwit, ur d-irennu  iɣallen 
d ifadden n ṭṭṛad. 
Di lawan deg Buxuc yesselqam awal netta d Sulla, nekk lhiɣ-d 
di  tfellaḥt-iw.  Yal  ass  anda  ara  yeɣli  yis-neɣ.    Nejjem  ad  nens 
sin wuḍan deg yiwem wemkan. Nedda d timzizzelt, yal tiɣremt 
nekcem  yiwen  wudem  i  nufa.  Imdanen  bedden,  heggan  i 
tnekra,  kkren  i  twizi  mgal  Aôumani.  Ɣas  irgazen  llan,  ɣas 
idamen  ḥman,    amur  ameqran  d  ifellaḥen.  Ifassen    yuɣen 
tannumi d uqabac akk d wanzel, ur zmiren azekka-nni kan ad 
ṣegmen  i  uneccab,  axtuc  neɣ  ajenwi.    Ur  zmireɣ  ad  megreɣ 
irgazen di tmura, ad ten-fkeɣ d asfel i ujenwi n Rruman. Abrid-
iw  nekk,  yal  ilemzi-nneɣ,  ilaq-as  ad  yekcem  ɣer  wennar 
imenɣi, ad yewwet, syin ad yeffeɣ d ameddur.  Riɣ ad ilin d wid 
ara yewwten, mačči d wid a yemten. 
Zegreɣ asif n Melwen, kecmeɣ tamurt n Buxuc. Yuzen-d ɣur-i 
ad  t-zreɣ.  Mi  nemlal,  yefka-yi-d  anda  yessaweḍ  awal  gar-as  d 
Marius.  Netta  yessarem  ad  naf  tawwurt  i  tifrat.  Yenna-yi-d :  
« Iôumaniyen  fkan-d  udem  akken  yal  yiwen  ad  yaɣ  abrid  n 
telwit ; ma neqqim, nezmer ad nefru uguren yellan gar-aneɣ ; 
ma neqqim-as, ur tella tindert ur nfessi ». 
Taggara,  buxuc  isegra-d  awal,  yenna-yi-d  :"Marius  yuzen-d 
Sulla    ad  nemlil  yid-s.  Abrid  n  tifrat  ad  t-id-naf  akken  yebɣu 
yentel.  Kečč  a  Yugurten,  ilaq-ak  ad  tôedbeḍ,  ad  tefsiḍ  tundar,  
ad d-tefkeḍ udem akken ad nekkes tazzla idammen gar-aneɣ d 
Rruman." 
Awal n Buxuc s webrid-is. Acu tettnadiḍ ay aderɣal, d tafat !

Carthage. Ih neɣ ala ? 
Buxuc  ur  iyi-d-yessefôez  tamsalt.    Akken  i  as-ddiɣ,  tagut 
simmal trennu teddal awal-is. Nekk, tiḥerci n Marius ssneɣ-tt, 
tin  n  Sulla  terna  tardast  ɣer  zdat.  Taggara  friɣ-as-tt  i  Buxuc, 
nniɣ-as : 
-  Nekni  akk  d  Rruman  am  tedyant-nni  "mmi-s  n  taɣaḍt  ad  t-
yečč wuccen".  Sulla yenna-ak ad yas. Nekk, yiwen webrid kan 
i  walaɣ  yessuffuɣ.  Sulla  ad  t-id-neṭṭef  gar  ifassen-nneɣ,  syin 
Iôumaniyen ad fken udem, am Marius am Senat di Ruma. Ma 
nurez-asen argaz am Sulla, nitni ad gen ayen nra nekni akken 
ad  asen-yuɣal  wergaz  d  ameddur.  Mi  neṭṭef  Sulla,  nezmer  ad 
ten-nesseks akken ad aɣen abrid nra nekni, ad ffɣen si tmurt-
nneɣ. Buxuc idhec. Abrid i as-d-wwiɣ ur yebni fell-as. Ur iyi-d-
yenna  zzant  neɣ  rɣant.  yessuter-iyi-d  ad  as-yewzen  i  tedyant 
kra n wussan ɣer zdat, syin ad tt-id-nefru. 
Nekk  uɣaleɣ-d  ɣer  wemkan-iw,  netta  ooiɣ-t  ad  yesseddu  awal 
netta d Sulla. Nefra ad yerr ɣuri kra wussan ɣer zdat. 
Timlilit-nni n Buxuc ur tris ɣef nniyya-w. Awal iyi-d-yessaweḍ 
Dabeô,  win  yellan  tama-s,  qbel  timlilit-agi  n  Buxuc  akk  d 
wawalen  n  Buxuc  s  timmad-is  netta,  fehmeɣ  tella  talast  gar-
asen. Ur ẓriɣ anida yella yiɣisi, ma d nekk, iɣisi-nni yella, ukiɣ-
as. Zrin kra n wussan, Buxuc yessaweḍ-iyi-d ad aseɣ tikkelt tis 
snat  ad  nefru  awal-nneɣ.  Acku  d  nekk  ara  izegren  ɣer  tmurt- 
is, yefka-yi-d amkan n temlilit, deg wasif n Melwen, talast gar 
Tamazɣa  d  Muriṭanya.  Nuɣ  abrid  nekk  akk  d  terbaât,  yid-neɣ 
ddan  sin  warraw-iw.  Mi  qrib  ad    naweḍ,  neẓra  s  lbaâd 
aḍeggal-iw Buxuc, ibedd ɣef yixef n tiɣilt netta d yimnayen-is. 
Yezger-d  i  wasif  akken  ad  aɣ-dyemmager.  Nekni  nesɣel-as, 
netta  yesɣel-aɣ-d  s  yiɣil-is.  Mi  nerna  tikli  ad  neddu  ɣer  zdat, 
qbel ad ten-naweḍ i d ɣlin fell-aɣ. yezzi-yaɣ-d weglaf n lâesker 
n Rruman.  Llan neṭlen  i tmuɣli, akin ddaw udernu. 
Nekni  nella  ifassen-nneɣ  d  ilmawen.  Ur  yella  s  wayes  ara 
newwet.  Rruman  nɣan  akk  wid  yellan  yid-neɣ.  Negra-d,  nekk 
akk d sin warraw-iw. Qqnen-aɣ tixelxalin n wuzzal.

Tikli n Ruma34 
D tannumi n Rruman : yal argaz ara yesmeɣren tamurt-
nsen  akin  i  tlisa  yellan,  nitni  ad  as-gen  tameɣra  tameqqrant 
(Triumphum) di tlemmast n Ruma. 
Tameɣra-nni deg-s sin wudmawen, tebrek temlel : d tameɣra i 
at  Ruma,  d  tanṭelt  i  wid  yettwarzen,  cudden  s  txelxalin  n 
wuzzal, ddan di tlemmast n lâeskeô. 
Ussan n tegrest  yezdeɣ-iten usemmiḍ. 
Tewzel  n  wussan-nni  trennu  amur  i  teɣzi  n  wuḍan  akken  ad 
sebken idammen, ad yeqqar weglim, ad kkawen ifadden. 
Asemmiḍ n Ruma yeqseḥ, di tegrest yerna tardast ɣer zdat. 
Campus Martius35, agni-nni yellan di tlemmast n Ruma, deffir 
ugadir,    yeččuô  d  imdanen,  yeččur  d  igemren,  d  izgaren  seg 
wacḥal  n  wussan  aya.  Imezdaɣ-nni  n  Campus  Martius  d 
34 Dans la Rome Antique, le Triomphe (Triumphum), c'est  la procession accomplie 
au  temple  de  Jupiter  Capitolinus  par  un  gẓnẓral  ḍainqueur.  …  le  triomphateur 
richement ḍḥtu et couronnẓ de lauriers, traḍersait la ḍille montẓe sur un char attelẓ 
de  quatre  cheḍaux  blancs.  L'armẓe  criait  "io  triumphe"  et  chantait  des  chansons 
paillardes. Suiḍaient les membres du Sẓnat, les magistrats, les prisonniers, le butin 
et les animaux destinẓs au sacrifice. Le cortège partait du Champ de Mars, hors les 
murs, entrait dans Rome par la porte triomphale, traḍersait le Circus maximus, 
contournait  le  Palatin,  aḍant  d'emprunter  la  Voie  sacrẓe  pour  atteindre  le 
Capitole.  Parḍenu  au  Temple  de  Jupiter,  le  gẓnẓral  immolait  lui-mḥme  les 
animaux destinẓs aux sacrifices et offrait sa couronne de lauriers au dieu.... 
Ce dẓfilẓ ẓtait attribuẓ par le Sẓnat romain, et constituait une rẓcompense pour le 
gẓnẓral  ḍictorieux.  Il  pouḍait  aḍoir  lieu  longtemps  après  sa  campagne.  Un  des 
critères  importants  ẓtait  le  butin  rapportẓ,  maca  il  ne  pouḍait  y  aḍoir  de 
triomphe  si  l'ager  romanus,  le  territoire  de  la  Rẓpublique,  n'aḍait  pas  ẓtẓ 
augmentẓ. 
35 Campus Martius  (Champ de Mars) / Annar n Meɣres, beôôa ugadir n Ruma.

imezdaɣ  n  tmara.  Ur  llan  d  wid  yetturaren,  ur  llan  d  wid  d-
yusan  ad  nezhen  uraren  n  circus  Flaminius  neɣ  circus 
Maximus,  deffir  tawant,  deffir  učči  yelhan  akk  d  tissit  n 
waman n waḍil. Imdanen-nni qqimen d tikemmucin, ssusmen,  
lâesker  n  Rruman  itezzi-asen,  teddun  akka  d  wakka,  afus  ɣef 
ujenwi neɣ uneccab. 
Urar deg wennar n Campus Martius di tegrest useggas -104 ur 
yella  d  win  ssnen  akk  imezdaɣ  n  Ruma.  Urar-nni  i  yasen-d-
ihegga Consul Marius i at Ruma, ira ad yili d win ɣef ara cfun 
iseggasen  d  iseggasen,  d  win  ara  ḥekkun  yemdanen  i  tarwa- 
nsen, i warraw n warraw-nsen, si lqern ɣer lqern. Akken i t ira 
Marius. 
Acḥal  n  wussan  si  mi  yeččuô  wennar  n  Campus  Martius.  Yal 
ass  rennun-d  yemdanen,  igemren,  izgaren.  Mi  d-tekcem  tissi 
ad taɣ amkan-is akin di teɣmert i as-heggan lâeskeô-nni. 
Tasusmi n wennar-nni trennu aɣilif ugar i wemkan-nni. Taduli 
n  tigugemt  tewweḍ  ula  d  izgaren  akk  d  iserdan-nni.  Üṣut  i  d 
yulin si Campus nni, tikwal d win kan n lâesker-nni i yezzin i 
wegraw,  neɣ  d  astenten  n  txelxalin  n  wuzzal.  Tixelxalin-nni 
yurzen irgazen wa ɣer wayeḍ. Asemmiḍ-nni n tegrest n Öuma 
yesberber-asen, yesdukel imdanen-nni, idel taduli n tsusmi fell-
asen. 
Acḥal  n  wussan  si  mi  yeččur  wennar-nni.  Laẓ  d  uṣemmiḍ 
kecmen  iɣsan  n  yemdanen.  Tiɣimit-nni  n  yal  ass,  si  tsebḥit  ar 
tmeddit,  si  tmeddit  ar  tsebḥit,  tessekref-iten,  laẓ  d  usemmiḍ 
yerna-yasen. Qqimen feclen. 
Ɣas serden,  ur uysen, ssarmen ad tbeddel fell-asen, am akken 
nnan  imezwura :  "akken  triḍ  ɣezzifeḍ  a  yiḍ,  taggara  ad  yali 
wass". Tikwal dɣa ssaramen ad yas wass deg ara tefru fell-asen, 
ad yeffeɣ yiṭij, ad yekkes uɣemɣum-nni deg llan. Melmi ara d-
yas wass ssaramen ? 
Imdanen-nni yeqqnen am wakraren ur llan d imezdaɣ n Ruma, 
ur  llan  d  imezdaɣ  n  Latinium,  n  Liguria,  neɣ  n  tmura  n 
Rruman  i  d  yezzin  akin.  Nitni  usan-d  si  tmurt  yellan  akin  i 
yilel, akin i waman izegzawen. Usan-d nnig lebɣi-nsen, ur llan 
d inebgawen n Ruma.

wwḍen,  rsen  seg  ubabuô-nni,    yuli-ten-id  lfeôḥ.  Nnan-as,

ččan-t  wuccanen  akin  i  yilel,  wa  ččan-t  waman  mi  d  zegren.

nsen.

useklu  ibedden  ...  Win  srewlen  iḍaôôen-is  yenser,  wid  urzen 
am nekni, cudden-aɣ-d, i kečč amek ? 
-  Ufan-aɣ-d  nkerrez,  akken  kan  yuli  wass.  Ini  si  mi  nebda 
takerza, nefôeḥ teswa-d, akal yerḍeb. Iḍelli-nni kan i zwaren i 
tkerza  At  Ufella.  D  nitni  si  zik  n  zik  i  d  yessufuɣen  tagersa  d

iɣrem-nneɣ.  Nekni  neqqen  tayuga  ad  nmeggel  taferka,  iṭij

n  tmes,  ččan-tt,  nekni  rran-aɣ  icuddan-nni,  qqnen-aɣ  zun  d 
izgaren-nni.  Taggara,  anzel  yuɣal  i  nekni.  Ijreḥ  wul-iw  ɣef 
tyuga-nni.  Yiwen  wezger,  win  yesâan  tarqemt  taberkant  gar

taggara  uɣen  tanumi  i  sin,  myussanen,  kerrzen  nebla  awal.

tefrut n Rruman !

yezgaren imellalen derren akin ;  d izgaren am tyuga-nni-nneɣ.

zzegren. 
Di tama niḍen n wennar, 
- I kečč ? 
-  Neẓra  Iôumaniyen  teddun-d.  Mi  wwten  ad  kecmen  tiɣremt, 
nekni  neffeɣ-d  si  tama  nniḍen ;  nezzi-asen-d,  nexdem  afernas 
deg-sen, ulac win inesren seg-sen d ameddur. Nɣil tefra. Mazal 
nessers uzzal, mazal tekkaw tidi fell-aɣ, mi d yerna wehdum n 
lâesker-nsen,  d  aweṭṭuf  neɣ  ugar  ;  yal  tama  tefka-d  ;  mačči  d 
ayen ara nqabel. Taggara n tedyant, iɣrem yuɣal d ixerban, wid 
nɣan mmuten, nekni qqnen-aɣ-d am izamaren... 
- I kečč amek teḍra ? 
-  Mi  yuli  wass  i  d  neẓra  udmawen  n  Rruman  nnig  ugadir  n 
yiɣrem; zzin-d i tuddar nekni ur sen-nuki ; iɣrem-nneɣ yenṭel 
di  teɣzut,  nɣil  ur  aɣ-d-ttawḍen,  taggara  ufan-d  anda  nezdeɣ  ; 
ur  aɣ-ooan  ad  naki.  D  asduqqes  i  aɣ-d-sduqqsen  seg  wusu  ; 
llan  wid  snin  s  ujenwi-nsen  akken  llan  deg  wussu  yeḥman. 
Azgen nɣa-t, azgen cudden-t-id... 
- Nekni, mi nesla yusa-d Rruman, neffeɣ seg yeɣrem, neffer deg 
yiger anda i nenṭel. Neqqim dinna kra wussan, nɣil tezri tyita, 
zegren  akin.  Taggara  mi  d  nezzi  ad  nekcem  ɣer  yiɣrem  nufa-
ten-id  ggunin  tawwurt;  ur  yella  wanda  ara  nerwel,  nekcem 
deg  umeôdax  ;  fernen  imeẓyanen,  wid  izemren,    rran-aɣ-d 
isuka  n  yirden  ɣef  izugar-nneɣ,  nedda  yid-sen.  Wiyaḍ  yečča-
ten ujenwi, zdat wallen-nneɣ. 
- Nekni nella neɣɣaz anu n waman. Acḥal n wussan nesalay-d 
tiquftin n wakal si ddaw tmurt. Nɣez tiddi n wergaz d wergaz, 
nnig  snat  temrawin  iɣallen.  Win  yellan  deg  wadda  ur  d-isel  i

ukessar ; lliɣ ɣɣazeɣ,  taquffet deffir wetma-s, wid yellan tama 
ufella  ssalayen-d  akal.  Tiremt  tis  snat,  nekk  uliɣ-d,  yuder 
Oendeô.  Yeffel  yiṭij  akin  i  yiɣil  mi  d  yeɣli  fell-aɣ  weglaf  n 
Rruman.  Yal  tama  tettefk-d  amur-is.  Nekk  d  Wakli  akk  d

Ëemmu,  zzin-aɣ,  ṭṭfen-aɣ,  fkan-aɣ  ayen  i  umi  zemren  n  tyita,

Yal  yiwen  tadyant  i  d  yeḥka,  yal  wa  d  aɣilif  i  t-yecqan  ;  wa 
yeooa-n tarwa-s akin i yilel, wa yeẓẓad deg wallaɣ-is tamuɣli-
nni  n  wid  yeglalzen,  mmuten  zdat-s  deg  wasif  idammen.  Yir 
tallit, yir taggara ! 
Imdanen  qqimen,  qqumcen,  ggunin,  tiddi  ur  tella.  D  amured 
kan  di  snat  turdas-nni  deg  llan  i  ubeddel  n  tmeûûaḍt.  Win 
yewwten ad yekker neɣ ad ibedd am akken bedden yemdanen, 
at  sin  iḍaôôen,  din  kan  ad  t-id-taweḍ  tyita  ɣer  wallaɣ,  neɣ 
aneccab  ger  yedmaren.  Si  tazwara-nni  mi  d  kecmen,  sin  seg-
sen i yessuffɣen seg wennar d iɣerrusen, yekka-asen uneccab si 
tama ɣer tayeḍ, mmuten din. Wid d yegran kerfen, uɣalen ɣef 
tgecrar.  Ifen-ten  igemren-nni  d  yezgaren-nni  izeggaɣen  d 
imellalen, nitni meqqar zemren ad qimen, ad bedden. 
Yir  rriḥa  tuɣ  akk  annar.  Ger  tuffɣa  n  yemdanen  akk  d  tin  n 
waxfiwen,  tazefrant-nni  trennu  teqseḥ  yal  ass.  Lâesker  n 
Rruman  simmal  rennun  teddun  akin,  simmal  rewwlen  akin, 
ɣunfan rriḥa n yemdanen-nni, rriḥa n wufni.  
Acḥal d ussan i yezrin, imdanen-nni ggunin tafat ansi ara sen-
d-tas. Deg wass amcum, qbel ad yali wass i yekker herwel deg 
wennar Martius. 
Asuɣu-nni  n  lâeskeô  n  Rruman  ad  yessaki  win  yemmuten. 
Teddun, afus yekkat, iḥebbek  akka d wakka, win yeqqimen ad 
yekker,  win  yemmuten  ad  yekker,  win  ur  nezmir  ad  t-yečč 
ujajiḥ. Akken llan  yemdanen-nni neggzen, bedden nnig lebɣi-
nsen.  Bedden  yir  tiddi  deffir  acḥal  n  wussan  n    uqummec,  n 
tikerfi.  Tagecrirt  tenṭeq,  taweṭzit  tsuɣ,  tiqesrit  tsuɣ.  Win 
yewwten  ad  yeqqim,  din  ara  t-id-taweḍ  tyita  n  wanzel  n 
Rruman. Ur tella tasa, ur yella yillu. 
Si  teqreḥ-nni  n  zellum  usemmiḍ,  iɣsan  saḥen,  igelman 
ddubzen,  tiddi  n  yemdanen-nni  tmal,  tekna  am  terga  uɣanim 
deg wass n waḍu. 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
Tagut-nni yedlen i Campus Martius tettifrir, tafat n wass trennu 
aɣilif ugar s wudmawen-nni akk d wallen-nni-nsen, udmawen 
n  laẓ  d  uɣilif.  Tban-d  tafat  ad  tekkes  tillas,  ad  teffeɣ  tiṭ  akin  i 
tmuɣli, taggara d tafat-nni i d-irennun tillas si tmuɣli taberkant 
n  yemdanen  icudden,  imdanen  yeknan  ur  d  tewwiḍ  tizi  n 
tewser. 
Asuɣu,  aḥbak,  amdegger  ...  Yekker  herwel  deg  wennar.    Win 
yeqqimen  yekker,  win  yekkren  yeɣli,  win  yeddan  yečča  tiyita, 
terki  deg  wennar  amcum.  Imdanen  yellan  ɣer  zdat  derren, 
iqḍaren  derren,  Rruman,  anzel  deg  ufus,  teddun  tṣeggimen 
rennun adar zdat wayeḍ. Yuli wass mi bdan tikli. Teddun tikli 
taẓayant, imdanen-nni teddun ur ẓran anida teddun. 
Wid  yellan  seg-sen  ssnen  Ruma,  ẓôan  zdat-sen  Circus 
Flaminius. Ddan aḍar deffir wayeḍ, ur bedden zdat  circus nni.  
Urar, ass-a agemmad i tewwurt n circus i yella. Di tezribt-nni 
deg  teddun  yemdanen  icudden,  izgaren  derren,  igemren 
bubben iḥemblen d ibeônusen,  ur yella wawal, ur tella taḍṣa. 
Afrag ineccaben n lâesker-nni si yal tama yeksa fell-asen aɣilif. 
Di  circus,  di  lawan-is,  llan  wuraren,  tella  temzizzelt  n 
yigemren,  n  yemdanen.  Uraren  n  wass-a,  zdat  circus,  ur  ten-
ggunint twuɣa, ur ten-yegguni waḥḥay ! 
Imdanen zrin akin,  tasusmi taẓayant tdel deffir  i circus-nni. 
Aqḍar  n  yergazen,  gemren  d  yezgaren  ddan  abrid-nsen. 
Simmal  ass  iteddu,  simmal  imezdaɣ  n  Ruma  teffɣen-d  zdat 
yexxamen-nsen  ẓerren  "iddawen-nni",  imdanen  iberkaken 
uqerruy n Numidya i d-izegren ɣur-sen. Di tazwara, imezdaɣ-
nni  dehcen  kan,  syin  yekkes-asen  ukukru.    Imaziɣen-nni 
ẓerren  zdat-sen  cudden,  afrag-nni  n  lâesker-nsen  yerna-asen 
tirugza.  Taggara,  ur  qqiment  tsusaf,  ur  yeqqim  yir  wawal,  ur 
yeqqim  ubuôôem  s  waṭṭiwen,  ur  yeqqim  wesɣal  s  yiɣil  ɣer 
imeḥbas-nni.  Imdanen-nni icudden, teddun aḍar deffir wayeḍ, 
ssusmen,  ur 
tisusaf-nni,  ur  d-sulin  aqerruy-
nsen… Akken triḍ ɣezzifeḍ a yiḍ, taggara ad yali wass …

nsen akin. Akken i tella si zik-nsen. Anekcum ɣer Ruma, ad yili 
s  yifassen  d  ilmawen,  d  anekcum  n  telwit-Mi  ten-tefka 
tewwurt-nni,  tiwuɣa  n  yimezdaɣ  n  Ruma  simmal  rennunt, 
ifergan  n  yemdanen  si  yal  tama  n  tzerbatin  simmal  iḍerres ; 
ɣursen  d  ass  n  tmeɣra.  Ɣas  tawwurt-nni  n  "Triomphe"  deg-s

Tikli-nni di tlemmast n Ruma, gar tsusaf d yir awal, tuɣal-asen 
d  tamagirt.  Ssarmen  ad  telli  tewwurt  ddaw  iḍaôôen-nsen,  ad 
ten-tečč tmurt akken llan, ad sgunfun. 
Teddun tikli n tmara,  tiwuɣa simmal rennunt ugar zdat-nsen. 
Nitni teddun ɣer zdat, awal-nni iteddu seg yiwen ɣer yiwen ɣer 
deffir : 
-  "Agellid-nneɣ,  Yugurten,  atan  ɣer  zdat  ;  icudd  am  nekni  ... 
agellid-nneɣ ... Yugurten, icudd s wuzzal, iteddu zdat-neɣ, akin 
deffir ucaôiḍ n Marius… llan warraw-is di sin...". 
Win yeslan i wawal-nni ad yiwriɣ wudem-is, syin ad yesseddu 
awal-nni  i  wid  d-iteddun  deffir.    Awal  iteddu  si  tmeẓẓuɣt  ɣer 
tmeẓẓuɣt, yuɣ idurra-nni iteddun tikli n taggara. 
Deg yixef n terḥilt ɣer zdat, Yugurten iteddu ger sin ifergan n 
lâesker,    uzzal  yeqqen  iḍaôôen  d  ifassen.  Deffir  teddun  sin 
warraw-is, cudden am netta. 
Yugurten iteddu tikli taẓayant. Ɣer zdat, akin, iban-as-d Marius 
ibedd s ubeônus-is, iteddu ɣef ucaôiḍ i jebdent snat tyugwin n 
yigemren  imellallen.    Yugurten  yekna  i  tuyat-is,  iteddu  aḍar 
deffir wayeḍ. Ur yesla i twuɣa, ur iwala iɣallen d-yesɣalen ɣur-
s, ur yeẓra arquqen i t-id-ibeômen. Iteddu, isers aṭṭiwen-is, am 
zun di targit i yella. 
Abrid yezzi, tarḥilt tezra zdat Forum Boarium38, syin tuɣ abrid  
37 « Le triomphe : le parcours du cortège est immuable, considẓrẓ comme un retour à 
la ḍie ciḍile des soldats citoyens. En franchissant le pomœrium, le gẓnẓral ḍainqueur 
abandonne  son  pouḍoir  de  commandement  militaire  (imperium),  symbole  de  son 
retour  à  sa  condition  de  simple  citoyen.  Partant  du  Champ  de  Mars,  où  les 
lẓgionnaires  dẓposaient  les  armes,  se  dẓtournant  symboliquement  du  dieu  de  la 
guerre ».

Imdanen-nni  iteddun  deffir  ttun  tilufa  deg  llan.  Si  mi  slan 
agellid-nsen, Yugurten, yella gar-asen, yettwaqqen ula d netta,

ass-a yeqqen am yiɣid, gar lâesker n Rruman, yir taggara !". 
Awwah ! Ur tezmir ad tili  tagi. Gguman ad amnen. 
Mi  d  ffɣen  si  circus  Maximus,  ddan  ɣer  zelmeḍ  zzin  i  tiɣilt  n 
Palatinum. Teddun tikli n tmara ur ẓran anida teddun. Ma ɣer

iteûûren.  Teddun  di  Ruma  am  zun  di  tlemmast  n  tesna  n 
warẓen. 
Iôumaniyen  simmal  sseḍyaqen-d  abrid,  simmal 
qerrben-d  iɣallen-nsen  d  yifassen-nsen  ɣer  udmawen-nsen. 
Tikli  simmal  tettiɣzif  mi  as-zzin  i  tewrirt  n  Palatinum,  syin 
uɣen  tazribt  tameqqrant,  Via  Sacra,  di  tlemmast  n  Forum 
Romanum. 
Tikli n luḍa, ɣas ma ifadden kkawen, ɣas ma ifadden cudden s 
ixelxalen  n  wuzzal,  amdan  yezmer  ad  yesseddu  iman-is,  aḍar 
deffir wayeḍ, ad yefk llu i tiddi-s.  Ɣas allaɣ sellaw si laẓ, ẓẓay 
seg  usemmiḍ  d  unezgum,  imdanen-nni  teddun  d  tissi,  win 
imalen  ad  as-d-gen  taôkizt,  ad  t-id-allen  watmaten-is.  Teddun 
deg webrid ur ssinen, di tmurt ur ssinen. 
Mi bdan tikli usawen di tezribt n Via Sacra, ukin i tgecrar-nsen 
feclent.  Abrid ibeddel, teddun yekkat-iten wugur ger teblaḍin-
nni  tizegzawin  n  Via  Sacra.  Tiwuɣa  simmal  rennunt-d,  abrid 
yetti, yerna ɣezzif ɣer zdat. Ɣas d aṣemmiḍ, amur seg-sen  d tidi 
n tkuffirt  tettqiṭṭir deg udmawen-nsen. Ur tella tiddi, ur yella 
wesgunfu.  Yal  yiwen  seg-sen  yeẓra  anda  ara  as-teffeɣ  i  win 
ibedden, i win yeɣlin yesred ur yezmir ad yeddu. Tuddma-nni 
ddmen lâeskeô winna yeɣlin di Tewwurt n Triumphum teqqim 
Bocca  della  Verita")  >  Circus  Maximus  >  Palatin  (yezzi  i  tewrirt  n)  >  Via  sacra

di  tmuɣli-nsen.  Tuddma-nni  kan  tefka-d  udem  s  anda  iteddu

Marius : « io triomphe ! ». 
Targit deg yella Yugurten, tefka anza i targit-nni n win yellan 
deg yifri n teryel. Targit akk d takwayt dduklent, ur tella talast 
gar-asent. 
Acḥal  n  wussan  yezrin  si  mi  t-id-ṭṭfen  Rruman.    Ussan-nni  n 
tubeô, ɣlin-d waman di lawan-is, teswa-d dɣa, llan wid ikerzen. 
Yella yessaram ad mɣin yigran, ad ččarent tesrafin n yirden d 
temẓin, ad yesdukel tamurt i tnekra tameqqrant, taggara tunef, 
tmal, yewwet wesyax di tlemmast. 
Tikli-nni  yuki-as  ɣezzifet.  Abrid-nni  deg  iteddu,  ɣas  d  iberdan 
yessen  si zik, ass-mi d yusa acḥal n tikkal ɣer Ruma, ass-a ur 
as-yufa udem. Ruma-nni yessen, ass-a tenger. Tiwuɣa-nni akk 
d  yir  awalen-nni  n  wid  yeččuôen  iberdan    kksen  sser  ɣef 
teɣremt n Ruma. Ruma d yekkan nnig akk tmura ! 
Yugurten iger tamuɣli akka d wakka ma ad ɣlint wallen-is ɣef 
yiwen  neɣ  sin  ger  wid  yessen  dinna,  wid  ukud  yečča  tagella. 
Yufa  ur  yella  din  yiwen.  Udmawen  n  wid  i  as-d-yezzin  ass-a 
cuban  wid-nni  n  yifri  n  teryel,  udmawen-nni  n  tmucuha. 
Ruma-nni n zik tenger, tucka. 
Abrid usawen di Via Sacra simmal yettiɣzif, simmal yessuddum 
am  zun  d  tinifift,  tikwal  d  asawen  tikwal  d  akessar.  Imdanen 
teddun  nehhten,  ifadden  kennun,  tiddi  tzelleg.  Wid  yellan  di 
tlemmast  feclen,  lâesker  yellan  di  tama  teddun  s  teḍṣa,  aḍar 
afessas,  udem  yennecôaḥ.  Abrid-nni  yessuddmen  iban-asen  i 
nitni d azaɣar. 
Tafat  n  yiṭij  n  tegrest  simmal  trennu,  wid  iteddun  s  tmara 
ɣezzifet fell-asen tiremt. Lemmer ẓran anida teddun, zemren ad 
as-gen ul, ad ṣebôen i dderk, i laẓ, i leâtab. Zemren ad ṛekḍen 
ɣef  ul-nsen,  ad  qeblen  leâtab-nni,  laẓ  d  usemmiḍ-nni,  taggara 
ad awḍen s anda teddun. Ad awḍen, ad tefsi tiyersi fell-asen, ad 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
sgunfun. Imdanen n tikli di Ruma, ur ten-id-yewwiḍ wawal, ur 
qdicen  i  tikli-nsen.  Amdan  icudden  s  ixelxalen  n  wuzzal,  ur 
yeqqim d amdan i tiṭ n win i t icudden. Si tallit-nni deg yicudd, 
am  zun  yeffeɣ  si  lufeq  n  yemdanen,  ikcem  addaynin  n  war 
amdan.  Akka  !  Timanit,  tanefsit,  tezmer  ad  tuɣal  d  urar  ger 
ifassen n yemdanen, ger ifassen  n wid d yuɣen tama ufella. 
Yiwen  seg  wid  yezwaren  ɣer  zdat,  tama  tazelmaṭ,  imal  abrid 
neɣ  sin,  syin  yuɣal-d.  Yerna  yedda  ɣer  zdat  aḍar,  yefcel, 
tigecrar  rgagint,  yerna  yedda  ɣer  zdat  asurif  neɣ  sin.  Mi  d-
degren  wid  yellan  deffir-s  ad  t-id-arzen  s  iɣallen-nsen  i  asen-
yenser.  Abrid  yeḍyeq  yessuddem.  Argaz  yewwi  tiɣiɣit  akin, 
yemrehwal  akka  d  wakka,  yenṭer  s  lqedd-is,  yesred.  Tikufta 
timellalin  ffɣent-d  seg  yimi-s.  Mazal  ters  tergagit-nni  mi  t-id-
wwḍen, ɣlin-d fell-as am zun d igudar. Lâesker zzuɣren argaz-
nni  am  zun  d  aceṭṭiḍ.  Sin  seg  yifassen,  sin  seg  yiḍaôôen, 
sdergen-t akin deffir ugadir. 
Nnig  wid  yellan  zdat-s  akk  d  wid  yellan  deffir-s,  argaz-nni 
yufeg,  yucka,  ur  t-yeẓra  yiwen.  Yeffeɣ  si  tmeddurt,  zun  ur  d 
ilul, ur yuzzil, ur yeḍṣa, ur yennuɣna. Ass-mi d-ilul di taddart-
nsen,  di  Tewrirt,  di  Tberka  neɣ  deg  Yiɣil  Imula,  ass-en  tefôeḥ 
yemma-s, slalwent-as tlawin di taddart, gant-as urar armi yuli 
wass. Ayen akk tessarem yemma-s, ayen akk yuzzel netta akken 
ad yuɣal d argaz, taggara yenɣel deg wass-nni n tubeô mi t-id-
urzen Rruman. Ass-a yesred di tegrest, deg webrid n Via Sacra, 
abrid yulin ɣer Capitolinus, di tlemmast n Ruma.² 
Ur yuli wass mi d-suffɣen Yugurten si lḥebs deg yella di Ruma. 
Usan-d  ɣur-s  d  aglaf  n  lâeskeô,  zzin-as,  ssulin-t  ɣef  ucaôiḍ  i 
zzuɣren  sin  igemren.  Ssuffɣen-t-id  akken  s  wuzzalen-nni 
yurzen iḍaôôen d ifassen. Yugurten iteddu s leḥder lemmer ad 
yeɣli, yewwet ad yali s ufella ucaôiḍ-nni. 
Ɣas akken argaz yeqqen, lâesker-nni zzin-as am wareẓẓen, gan 
afrag,    afus  ɣef  ujenwi  neɣ  ɣef  uneccab.  Ur  yella  wawal  ger 
Yugurten akk d wid d yusan ɣur-s. 
Tamuɣli-nni  n  tewwurt  n  Triumphum  tefka-as-d  tasarut  n 
tuffɣa  i  t-id-yessuffɣen  taûebḥit.  Tikkelt-agi  yeẓra  mačči  ɣer 
tmettant i t-id-srekben. 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
Mi  yeẓra  anect-nni  n  lâesker,  anect-nni  n  yimeḥbas,  n 
yigemren, n yizgaren d wayen icudden s ufella n icaôiḍen-nni, 
yefhem anwa i d abrid-is. 
Yugurten yessen Iôumaniyen, yessen Ruma am zun d tamurt is. 
Acḥal n tikkal i yezger ilel, yerzef ɣer Ruma. Dɣa si tedyant-nni 
n  ṭṭṛad  n  Numance  iga-d  imeddukal  ugar,  imeddukal-nni  n 
tidet,  wid  yellan  ɣer  tama-s,  wid  ukud  idegger  lâesker  n 
Numance. 
Ameddakel  yellan  di  tizi  n  tḍiq,  di  tizi    n  tidet  anda  ɣellin 
yergazen,  yiwen  ur  yezmir  ad  t-yettu.  Di  tedyant-nni  dɣa  i 
yuki,  yekcem  di  tlemmast  n  yidles  aôumani  ;    yessen  amek 
teddun,  amek  ẓerren  tameddurt,  timmanit-nsen  ;  yessefra-d 
ayen yezwaren ɣur-sen d wayen yegran ɣur-sen.  Mi ara yili di 
tlemmast  imeddukal-is  Iôumaniyen,  yettaki  i  yiman-is  zun  d 
yiwen  seg-sen,  d  Aôumani  am  nitni  ;  ayen  yelhan  yessen-it, 
ayen ur nelhan yessen-it. Tikwal dɣa yessaram ad yas wass deg 
ara yesdukel ayen yelhan ɣur Rruman akk d wayen yelhan ɣur 
Yimaziɣen am netta akken ad yebnu tamurt akken i tt-imenna 
netta.  Di tallit-nni deg yella baba-s Makawsen d agellid, tikwal 
iẓer  tagelda  n  Sirta  abrid-is  ɣer  deffir  mačči  ɣer  zdat.  Llant 
tikwal dɣa deg yessaram ad yuɣal jedd-is Masensen, ad yuɣal d 
ilemẓi  akken  ad  as-ibeddel  abrid  i  tmurt.    Tikwal  dɣa  mi  ara 
iẓer  ilmeẓyen-nni  di  Sirta,  i  yecban  Aderbal,  Gawda  akk  d 
wiyaḍ, wid akken d-yekkren di leḥrir d taḍuḍt, rennun wurfan 
deg-s  ugar.  Di  lawan  i  deg  yelmeẓyan  n  Rruman  ur  sgunfun 
ger tazzla s wegmer, almad imenɣi s ujenwi d uneccab, tazzla 
ɣef uḍar, wid-nneɣ sbuḥrun-asen waklan ddaw tara tazegzawt 
di tewririn n Sirta. Abrid-is netta, yeẓra ur yella d abrid-nsen. 
Tallit-nni  mi  sbedden  acaôiḍ  zdat  tewwurt  n  Triumphum, 
imezdaɣ  n  Ruma  ččuren-d  annar.  Awal  yeffeɣ  s  ɣur  lâesker-
nni, dɣa at Ruma bdan-d yir awalen ɣer wudem-is. 
Yugurten  yessen  amezruy  n  tikli  n  Triumphum  mačči  armi  d 
ass-a.  Si  zik  n  zik  yusa-d  jedd-is  Masensen  ɣer  Triumphum n 
Scipion, yusa-d Makawsen d inebgi. Ass-a lemmer  tṣeggem, ad 
yili d inebgi n Senat mačči d ameḥbus s wuzzalen... 
Ifhem  ass-a  d  ass  n  Triumphum  n  Marius.  D  ass-is  ilmend  n 
wayen d yessas i tmurt-is. 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
Isers  aqerruy-is,  ur  isel  i  yir  awal,  ur  yuki  i  tsusaf-nni  i  t-id-
yewwḍen  ;  ɣas    tafekka-s  tella  din,  allaɣ-is  yezger  akin  ɣer 
teɣremt  n  Sirta.  Ayen  akk  yezrin  si  lmut  n  Makawsen,  ass-a 
iban-as-d  am  tafat-nni  n  magu,  iban-as  yefren,  yufaf,  yektal, 
yuɣal  ɣer  tesga.  Triumphum  agi  iban-as-d  am  win  yufan 
tasarut-nni i as-idergen acḥal n wussan, acḥal n yiseggasen. 
Azal  ameqqran  n  Triumphum yessen-it  netta.  Yeẓra  anwa  i  d 
aẓar-is di tmurt n Rruman : akken ad ttili tikli n Triumphum i 
yiwen  seg  wid  yeseddan  ṭṭṛad,  i  jiniral  n  lâesker  i  yecban 
Marius,  ilaq  cceôt  ameqqran.  Ilaq-as  ad  yili  yerna-d  akal39 
akken ad yessemɣer, ad yessnerni tamurt n Rruman. 
Senat i as-d-iqeblen ass-a tikli-agi n Triumphum i Marius, ɣur-
s tefra. Marius yerna-d tamurt i Rruman, idegger akin tilisa n 
tmurt  n  Rruman,  yerna-d  Tamazɣa  (Numidya)  d  aḥric 
amaynut  i  Ruma.  Ɣur-sen  tefra,  seg  wass-nni  deg  d-ṭṭfen 
Yugurten,  Tamazɣa tuɣal d taferka-nsen. 
Afrag-nni  iga  Yugurten  yekkes-asen  i  Rruman  seg  wass-mi  t-
id-cudden s ixelxalen n wuzzal ! 
Yugurten iteddu, aḍar deffir wayeḍ, ur yesla i twuɣa, ur yuki i 
tsusaf. Aɣilif-nni ameqqran yellan fell-as yuki-as yettifsus. Ass-
a tefra-as-d. Anezgum-nni iga seg wass-mi yekker i ṭṭṛad mgal 
Rruman,  ass-a  yettifrir  am  tagut-nni  n  tefsut.  Akukru-nni  
yemmugger  acḥal  d  tallit,  di  yal  imenɣi,    ass-a  yekkes.  Yeẓra 
netta seg wass amezwaru deg webrid n tissas i yella.  Yennuɣ 
Rruman  acku  nitni  begsen  di  tazwara  ad  kecmen  Tamazɣa. 
Tamettant-nni  n  Makawsen  tusa-asen-d  d  tawwurt  akken  ad 
kecmen Sirta. Nitni heggan, begsen, cudden-tt, taggara ufan-d 
Yugurten d axsim-nsen. 
Abrid-nni  heggan-t  si  zik.  Heggan  arraw  n  Makawsen  akken 
ad  kerzen  yis-sen.  Lemmer  ur  ten-heggan  yili  Aderbal  ur  d 
yessuffuɣ  awalen-nni  zdat  tejmaât  n  Senat  ass-mi  yezger  ɣer 
Ruma akken ad yeccetki. Yenna-yasen ass-nni : "Tamurt d ayla-
nwen kenwi, nekni d iqeddacen-nwen ...". 
Afus deg-neɣ i yella. 
39  Triomphe : " Un des critères importants ẓtait le butin rapportẓ, maca il ne pouḍait 
y aḍoir de triomphe si l'ager romanus, le territoire de la Rẓpublique, n'aḍait pas ẓtẓ 
augmentẓ".  L’annexion de la Numidie se confirme !

Di  15  yiseggasen  imenɣi  mgal  Rruman,  llant  tikwal  anda 
Yugurten    iga  ccek.  Llant  tikwal  i  deg  yefcel.  Taggara,  yal 
tikkelt yettaf tazmert ɣer zdat, yettaf afud amaynut i tnekra. 
Yugurten  iteddu  s  taẓeyt,  knant  tuyat,    ger  tiwuɣa  d  uqejjem, 
allaɣ-is yunag akin ɣer wedrar n Awras, akin ɣer Sirta. 
Mi  d-yetkaki  ilmeẓiyen-nni  i  d-yemmugger  di  tikli-s  di  yal 
tiɣremt  n  Tmazɣa,  yeẓra  deg  wul-is  ass-a,  yeẓẓa  di  tmurt-is 
aẓar n tnekra. 
Yeẓôa  yessaɣ  tafat  n  tnekra  deg  wulawen-nsen.  Tafat-nni  ur 
nxessi. Yeqqen allen-is, iteddu am uderɣal, aḍar deffir wayeḍ. 
Ɣer zdat, Marius, s ufella ucaôiḍ amellal i jebdent snat tyugwin 
igemren  imellalen,  iteddu  ɣer  tewrirt  n  Capitolinus.  Iteddu 
akken  ad  yefk  lwaâda,  ad  yeẓẓal,  ad  yessizzel  idammen  i 
Jupiter. Ad as-yerr lxiô… 
Di Tullianum 
Mi  tewweḍ  tikli  n  triomphe  ɣer  Capitolinus,  Marius 
yeẓẓul taẓallit-is,  yessazzel idammen n yezgaren at wacciwen.  
Yewweḍ lebɣi-s. 
Imeḥbas  Imaziɣen  akk  d  wid  n  tmura  nniḍen,  nehôen-ten  ɣer 
iderbaz anda ttilin. Azekka-nsen yiwen, d aberkan : ad nzen d 
aklan-neɣ ad ten-yečč ujenwi neɣ yizem deg wuraren n circus 
di Ṛuman. Ffɣen si tudert. 
Yugurten ssudren-t ɣer lḥebs Mamertinum, d abrid ɣer tesraft 
n Tullianum, akin ddaw tewrirt n Capitolinus, deg yixef n Via 
sacra. 
Qbel  ad  gren  Yugurten  deg  yimi40  ufella  n  tesfrat-nni,  fsin-as 
tixelxalin-nni n wuzzal, kksen-as iceṭṭiḍen-is, rnan jerḥen-t mi 
as-d-qeccmen timengucin-nni n wureɣ seg yimeẓẓuɣen-is. 
Inṭer ɣer tlemmast n tesraft tasemmaḍt, d aâeryan akken i t-id-
turew  yemma-s.  Yenṭeô  ɣef  yeblaḍen,  imeẓẓuɣen  teddun  d 
idammen...  
I ɣezzifeḍ a yiḍ ! 
Tillas d usemmiḍ zedɣen tasraft-nni deg yekcem Yugurten. 
Tebrek  akk  d  yir  rriḥa  rennunt-as  ugar  aɣilif  i  wemḍiq-nni. 
Tasraft-nni  telli-d  imi-s  si  ddaw  tmurt  am  zun  d  talafsa.  Ur 
yuki mi d yufa iman-is yeglalez adda, di tlemmast n tesraft. Mi 
as-d-bran si tama ufella, ur yeẓra yeɣli-d ɣef uqerru-s neɣ ɣef 
iḍaôôen-is. Yeqqim, yenzef. 
40 Imi n tesraft n Tullianum yezzi, yenjer deg weẓru aberkan,  tehri-s (diamètre)   =  
0,61 m ; tiddi n tesraft  (hauteur) = 3,53 m (= 12 pieds romains) ; tehri-s azal n 3,5 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
Rriḥa-nni i t-id-yewwten ɣer tanzarin-is, tesmektay-as-d ifran-
nni  n  Taza,  ifran-nni  anda  zedɣen  yizmawen.  Yugurten 
yeccarrew.  yeẓẓel afus-is, yufa-t ẓẓay zun d azduz. Ɣas kksent 
txelxalin  n  wuzzal  i  t-yurzen  acḥal  n  wagguren,  yuki-as  i 
tesmeḍ-nni-nsent, yuki-as i taẓeyt-nni-nsent. Yemmekta-d anda 
yella. 
Akken yeqqim ur as-yufa udem. 
Teqseḥ-d  tesmeḍ  n  yeblaḍen-nni  gan-as-d  ineccaben  deg 
weksum-is. Yeẓẓel iḍaôôen-is, yufa yerra-t-id udernu n weẓru.  
Tigecrar qqiment kerfent. Iṣeggem iman-is. 
Ur yeẓôa llint wallen-is neɣ qqnent. Ur yeẓra amek i as-d-tegra 
i yeẓri-s.  Ur yeẓri d ass neɣ d iḍ, tezzint deg wallaɣ-is. Tebrek-
nni  n  tesraft  akk  d  tillas-nni  rnant  tidderɣelt  i  tidderɣelt. 
Yeqqim, yessusem. 
Yuki-yas  i  tesmeḍ  tuɣ  aglim-is.  Isers  afus-is  ɣef  yedmaren-is, 
yufa  ur  yella  uceṭṭiḍ,  ur  tella  tselsa.  Yegra-d  akken  d  ilul  si 
tâebbuḍt n yemma-s. 
Yesself i wudem-is, yuki i ufus-is yulwaɣ, yeḥma-d si tnalit-nni. 
Idammen  rennun  tazla  seg  yimeẓẓuɣen-is,  udren-d  d  akessar, 
gan-d targa ɣer tuyat-is. 
Yugurten yewwet ad yetkaki. Acḥal aya  i  yella di  tesraft-agi ? 
Imir kan ? D ussan, neɣ d aguren ? 
Ur d yufa. Xeôbent deg wallaɣ-is. 
Rriḥa-nni  tazefrant  n  tesraft  terna  tɣeẓẓa-t  ugar  di  tenzert-is. 
Rriḥa-nni  tesmekta-as-d  tadyant-nni,  ass-mi  yeḍfer  izem  nepa 
d yimeddukal-is, Ameqqran akk d Gider, di teẓgi n Taza, tiẓgi n 
wegdel deg wedrar n Awras. 
Yugurten  yetkaki  d  tedyant-nni,  iẓeô-itt,  zun  tella-d  zdat 
waṭṭiwen-is : 
-  "  ...  mi  aɣ-yenser  yizem-nni  tikkelt  tamezwarut,  neooa  din 
imeddukal,    wid  yeddan  yid-neɣ.  Nuzzel,  nuɣ  abrid  deg  yezri 
yizem-nni. Nedda acḥal, izem yufeg, yucka, ur d-iban lateô-is. 
Nezzi  i  teẓgi,  nekka-as  tama  ufella,  nerna  tama  n  wadda,  ur 
yella  yizem.  Nerna  tikli  ɣer  zdat,  syin  ners  ɣer  tmurt.  Neqqen 
igemren-nneɣ dɣa nedda ɣef  uḍar  gar  yisekla n wegdel akk d 
umadaɣ. 
Mi  nuli  asawen,  newweḍ  ɣer  yiwen  weslaḍ,  nufa  dinna  llan 
iceôfan, llan yefran. Negguni  tiremt,  ur  d  yenṭiq wefôux, ur d 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
ineggez wewtul. Tasusmi-nni tdel amḍiq-nni, tesberber-as zun 
d tasusmi-nni usalu n wedfel yessan. 
Ameqqran  akk  d  Gider  zzin-d  s-wadda,  nekk  lliɣ  tama  ufella. 
èôiɣ-ten mi bedden akin. Sseɣleɣ-asen s uneccab-inu akken ad 
asen-iniɣ : "nekk ad kecmeɣ ɣer yefri-nni yellan zdat-i, nitni ad 
bedden ɣef yiman-nsen". 
Gider  yerra-yi-d  s  yiɣil-is,  zun  akken  yenna-d  :  "kečč  zwir, 
nekni  ad  nergel  abrid  n  wadda".    Ddiɣ  snat  tsuraf  kan  gar 
yeblaḍen mi ɣliɣ ɣef yimi n yefri. Amruj-nni n yifri yella yeffer-
it udafal,yeḍres fell-as am zun d azeṭṭa. 
Yella deg wawal : "ifri n yizem, ɣas d ilem yessagad". 
Mi skecmeɣ aqerruy-iw di tewwurt n yifri iyi-d-tewwet rriḥa-
nni  ɣer  tenzarin-iw,  rriḥa-nni  taqesḥant,  tazefrant.  Mi  d-rriɣ 
iman-iw ɣer deffir akken ad nefseɣ abeḥri azedgan i d-ineggez 
kra zdat-i, yeffeɣ-d ger igenni akk tmurt, yufeg akin am waḍu 
ɣer  tama  n  teẓgi.  Imir,  nekk  ur  ẓriɣ  tigert.  Ukiɣ  kan  i  waḍu 
ameqran,  « huuufff ! Ukiɣ  i  kra  ihucc-iyi  akin,  icrew  iɣil-iw, 
syin iḍegger-iyi akin ɣer weslaḍ n tnicca. 
Mi d ukiɣ, ufiɣ-d iman-iw ẓleɣ ger yimeddukal-iw, Gider akk d 
Ameqqran,  aqerruy-iw  icudd  s  uceṭṭiḍ  n  tejbirt  umagraman. 
Mi  serseɣ  afus-iw  ɣef  uqerruy-iw,  ukiɣ  i  ḥamu  n  idammen-
nni...". 
Tesmeḍ-nni  n  tesraft  tebda  tkeččem  ugar  deg  yiɣsan  n 
Yugurten. Yeccarrew. Yesferfed i weksum-is, iḥukk iɣallen-is s 
ifassen-is  akken  ad  yesenɣes    tisuqqas  usemmiḍ-nni.  Tadyant-
nni  n  yizem  terna  deg-s  anezgum.  Yetkaki-d  imeddukal-is  n 
temẓi. Gider, Ameqran, anida llan  ass-a ? 
Di  tesraft-nni,  izirig  arqaq  n  tafat  i  d-yudren  akin  si  tegnawt 
yebda  iselles.    Iẓôa-nni  n  tesraft  i  as-d-yezzin  bdan  neṭlen 
yiwen yiwen.  Ur yefrin ma d ass i yeffalen akin i yiɣil am yal 
tameddit neɣ d iẓri-s nepa i umi ddalent tillas, yebda yettderɣil. 
Yeqqen  aṭṭiwen-is,  yefka  tameẓẓuɣt    ad  isel  i  wayen  i  as-d-
yezzin. Ur yella ûûut, ur yella wawal. Yuki i yiman-is yenṭel d 
ameddur. Tuli-d tkuffirt deg-s, inteq ɣer yiman-is : 
-  "  Nekk,  Yugurten  n  At  Yiles,  aqli  di  tesraft  n  Ruma,    neṭleɣ 
ddaw tmurt, ttwarzeɣ aḍar afus...". Di taɣect-is ur d yeffiɣ ûûut. 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
Yekref-d  tigecrar-is,  yesker 
iman-is  akken  ad  as-yenɣes 
usemmiḍ,  ma  d  allaɣ-is  yezger,  yunag  akin  i  yilel,  akin  i 
yidurar, akin i uzaɣar n tmurt-is. 
Yugurten  yerra  tamuɣli  ɣer  deffir,  ɣer  wussan  ineggura. 
Ussan-nni  tezzin  zdat  wallen-is,  tezzin  rennun  :  timlilit  n 
Tzaɣart, Buxuc, Sulla, Dabaô, Iôumaniyen zzin-as-d am wejôad, 
idammen, tisusaf, uzzal,  tixelxalin, yir awal... 
Yugurten yeṭṭef aqerruy-is ger ifassen-is, yewwet ad yekkes seg 
wallaɣ-is ayen akk iẓeô di tedyant deg yella, taggara imukan n 
txelxalin-nni n wuzzal aẓayan rrant-d tamuɣli-s ɣer wemkan-
nni  deg  yella.  Iḥuk  iɣallen-is,  yuki  mačči  d  targit  i  yettargu. 
Yerna  yesself  i  yifassen-is,  i  yiḍaôôen-is,  ur  yeẓôa  yella  neɣ  ur 
yella wuzzal-nni. 
Ayen  i  yesnedfen  ul-is  ugar  ur  yella  d  tadyant  yeḍran  yid-s, 
tufa-t-id ass-a yeṭṭef tama wadda zdat ucengu Aôumani. Tidet, 
nepa tuɣ-it yennum tilufa, yennum akessar d usawen, yennum 
uguren  seg  wass-mi  i  t-id-turew  yemma-s.  Isers  afus-is  ɣef 
yedmaren-is d tuyat-is, yesself i weksum-is, yuki i cwami-nni n 
tyitwin uneccab, tiyitwin ujenwi neɣ ucangal. Ɣas llant cwami-
nni  deg  weksum-is,  ɣur-s  am  zun  ur  llant.  Acḥal  imenɣiyen 
deg yella, deg yewwet, deg yečča tiyita, taggara yufrar-d di yir 
tallit. Ajraḥ n tyita s ɣur ucengu yeqqaz iḥellu... 
Ayen i yesnedfen ul-is ugar, d tiyita-nni i as-d-yekkan si deffir, 
seg yidammen-is. 
Yefka awal, yefka laman i  Buxuc akken  ad  yemlil nepa akk  d 
Sulla-Ad  mlilen  akken  ad  afen  tawwurt  n  tifrat  netta  akk  d 
Iôumaniyen,  Buxuc42  ad  yili  d  anagi.  Taggara  teffeɣ  tedyant 
akken nniḍen. 
Nekk ɣileɣ ad tili d timlilit n tifrat, d timlilit n Tzaɣart s ufus n 
Buxuc,  taggara  tuɣal  d  yir  targit.  Aḍewwal-is  yefka  afus  deg 
yidammen n warraw-is,  , yezzenz-it i Rruman. 
Akken  i  as-yewzen  Yugurten  ur  as-yufa  ixef-is.  Di  tazwara 
dduklen  netta  akk  d  Buxus,  sdukklen  tazmert-nsen  d  lâesker-
41 Cornelius Sulla : ilul di -138, tefka-t-id Ruma  di -108 (questeur)  ɣer Numidya n 
wegmuḍ, ddaw leḥkem n Marius. D nepa i d-yurzen Yugurten, s ufus n Buxuc. 
42 Buxus (Bocchus) : agellid n Muôetanya (Tamazɣa utaram / Meôôuk akk d tmurt n 
wehran n wass-a). 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
nsen,  nnuɣen  Iôumaniyen  di  yal  amkan,  di  Sirta  neɣ  anda 
nniḍen. Taggara tunef. 
Amek yewweḍ Buxuc ad yezzenz aḍewwal-is, ad t-iger gar  
tucar Iôumaniyen ? Yugurten ur as-yufa tawwurt. Yetkaki d  
awal-nni n zik : "tixsi d idammen-is i tt-yenɣan". 
Acḥal n Imaziɣen am nepa i d yegran di tesrafin neɣ di leḥbus 
n Rruman, mmuten neɣ nzan d aklan. Yugurten yufa ur yella d 
amezwaru  di  tedyant-agi.  Yetkaki  d  wid  akk  yellan  yid-s  deg 
yimenɣiyen,  wid  i  d-ṭṭfen  Iôumaniyen,  cudden-ten-id  d  aklan 
ɣer  tmurt-nsen.  yetkaki-d  daɣen  tadyant  n  ugellid  Sifaks43, 
yettwacudd am nepa di tmurt n Rruman. Yeṭṭef-it-id Masensen 
akk  d  Consul  Laelius  deg  yimenɣi  n  Sirta.  Sifaks  yemmut  d 
aɣrib di teɣremt n Tibur44, di tmurt n Rruman. Ɣas Sifaks yenfa, 
yekker-d mmi-s, Awernin45, yeseɣzef imenɣi mgal Masensnen. 
Tamurt Tamaziɣt teqqim tebḍa ɣef sin. 
Izirig-nni  n  tafat  di  tesraft  iselles.  Yugurten  yesker  iman-is  di 
teɣmert,  aqerruy  ger  ifassen,  yeqqim  yegguni.  Iger  tamuɣli  i 
yiseggasen ineggura i yezrin : 
-"Tadyant i aɣ-d-yessawḍen ɣer dagi, aẓar-is yella si zik n zik. 
Nuɣ  tannumi,  ar  d-yenɣel  ubuqal    i  nettuɣal  i  tuzzma.  Di  yal 
tallit,  ussan  yezrin  am  zun  ur  nessin  ad  nelmed  seg-sen.  Ɣur-
neɣ,  ayen  yezrin  yewwi-t  waḍu.  Yal  tikkelt  ad  as-nuɣal  s 
wadda am zun imir kan i d-nlul. 
Ugur  ameqran-nneɣ  :  nessemɣar  tin  yella  gar-aneɣ  armi  d 
tidderɣelt  deg  ur  nẓer  uguren  i  aɣ-d-yezzin,  uguren  n  tlisa, 
uguren n beôôa. Yal tikkelt akka. Win d-yusan si beôôa yezmer 
ad  yekrez  yis-neɣ  ma  yufa  tasarut  n  iceqqiq  yellan  deg-neɣ  : 
taɣennant-nni yellan gar-aneɣ si zik n zik. 
Ass-mi yemmut babat-neɣ Makawsen, ɣilleɣ wwḍen-d wussan 
deg nezmer a nbeddel udem i Tmazɣa. Nwiɣ ad as-neddukel i 
twizi  tameqqrant,  ad  nessaki  ilmeẓyen  n  tmurt,  ad  nebnu 
43  Agellid  Sifaks  (Syphax)  :  Yemmut  d  ameḥbus  di  tmurt  n  Rruman,  di  teɣremt  n 
Tibur.  D  Masensen  akk  Laelius    i  t-id-yeṭṭfen  di  Tmazɣa,  deg  yimenɣi  wis  sin  ger 
Carthage, di yiwet tama,  akk d Rruman d Yimaziɣen di tama nniḍen (2eme guerre 
punique).  Masensen imal ɣer  Rruman, Sifaks imal ɣer Carthage. 
44 Tibu, tura isem-is (TIVOLI), d tamdint  n Ïalyan, tezga-d 32 km  akin, agmuḍ (Est) n  
Rruman. 
45 Awernin = Vernina (s tlatinit), mmi-s n Sifaks. 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
tiɣremtin,  ad  nenjer  iberdan  imeqqranen,  ad  nɣez  tiregwa  d 
isaffen  i  waman  ad  awḍen  timura,  ad  swen  yegran.  Nɣil 
tamussni tella, iɣallen llan. Taggara teffeɣ targit tezleg. 
Yir tagmat tettôuẓ ifadden. Mazal yekkaw uẓekka n babat-neɣ  
Makawsen,  atmaten-iw  Hiemsal  akk  d  Aderbal  begsen  i  tlufa. 
Anda  ilaq  ad  nemyefk  tayet,  ad  nekker  i  tmurt,  nitni  heggan 
tifxet. D nekk, gmat-sen, i d ufan d acengu-nsen mačči d laẓ d 
cwal  yellan  ger  tmura  n  Tmazɣa.  Nitni  kkren-d  deffir  ugadir, 
di  liser,  d  tawant,  dɣa  tamuɣli-nsen  tuɣal-d  kan  ansi  d  yuɣal 
ugadir i asen-d yezzin di Sirta. Kkren-d deg wudi d tamemt, di 
taḍuḍt, ugaden ad asen-tekkes.  Ur ffiɣen, ur kcimen timura n 
Tmazɣa  neɣ  tid  n  medden,  ur  gan  imenɣi,  ur  ten-tuɣ  deg 
tedyant  anda  ara  rgagin  iɣesmaôen-nsen,  anda  ara  teffeɣ  seg-
sen tidi-nni tasemmaḍt. 
Anda ilaq ad cemôen i yiɣallen-nsen, nitni fran-tt ad qimen di 
ḥamu d tiẓeḍt n tamemt deg uɣen tannumi ass-mi yella babat-
nneɣ. 
Ass-mi  llan  di  tattalt,  am  Aderbal  am  Hiemsal,  nekk  nudaɣ 
Tamazɣa  seg  yixef  ɣer  yixef,  seg  wagmud  ar  utaram,  seg 
wanẓul ar ugafa. Zegreɣ isaffen, zegreɣ idurar, ulac tiɣremt ur 
kcimeɣ, ulac taddart ur ssineɣ. Anda kkiɣ d atmaten-iw, axxam 
kecmeɣ  d  axxam-iw.    Yal  tikkelt  s  mraw  ifassen  iyi-d-
ttmaggaren at tmurt-iw. 
Zegreɣ  ilel  ɣer  tmurt  n  Spanya,  kecmeɣ  di  ṭṭṛad  n  Numance, 
tama  n  lâesker  n  Rruman,  nemyefk  tayet,  nečča  aɣrum 
asemmaḍ,  necrew  tidi  d  idammen.  Imir  Iôumaniyen  llan  d 
imeddukal-nneɣ, mačči am ass-nni am ass-a… 
Di Numance, isem n Tmazɣa yuli-as yiseɣ. 
Deg  imenɣi,  anda  terki,  anda  tegguma  ad  tefru  tyita,  d  nekk 
wuɣur d-idellu Scipion. Mi nekcem annar, ad neg afernas deg 
ucengu.  Dinna  di  Numance,  nesdukel  tamussni-nneɣ  di  ṭṭṛad 
akk  d  tin  nelmed  ɣer  Rruman.  Nerna-d  afud  i  yiseɣ  n 
yelmeẓyen Imaziɣen i wwiɣ yid-i. Nefka ixef-nneɣ i wudem n 
yiseɣ n tmurt-nneɣ. 
Ass-mi  tefra  tin  n  Numance,  mi  nekker  ad  d-nuɣal,    zdat 
lâesker    d  yezzin  i  aɣ-d-yenna  Scipion  awalen  ineggura  : 
"kenwi  lâesker  n  Tmazɣa,  tefkam-aɣ-d  tayet,  tefkam  iqerray- 
nwen  i  tifrat  n  yimenɣi  n  Numance,  i  temɣer  n  Ruma. 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
Tzegrem-d  ilel  akken  ad  tegrem  afus  deg  yimenɣi  tama-nneɣ. 
Ass-a, azekka Ruma ur tettettu ayen tgam di tmurt dagi. ...". 
Neẓra awal n Scipion  anda yessaweḍ ass-a. 
Ass-mi d nuɣal si Numance, imeddukal-nneɣ yemmuten din ur 
ten-nettu.  Mi  d-nuɣal  kan,  nezzi-d  i  tmurt,  neẓra  imawlan  n 
yergazen  i  neooa-n  akin  i  yilel.  D  lmut-nsen  i  yernan  azal  i 
tmurt n Tmazɣa ; iseɣ ameqqran, d yidammen-nsen nitni i t-id- 
yewwin i Makawsen." 
Tasusmi-nni  yedlen  Tullianum    terna-d  amur-is  n  tebrek  i 
tillas, i taẓeyt uɣemɣum-nni. Idammen-nni sebken ɣef tuyat-is, 
rnan-d  tesmeḍ  i  weksum-is.  Yugurten  yekna,  iger  afus-is  ad 
yennal  ixelxalen-nni  n  wuzzal  i  t-yurzen.  Yesferfed  ifassen 
iḍaôôen ulac, ur llan ixelxalen-nni.  Yessarem ad ten-yaf akken 
ad ten-yeg d imwansen. 
Yuɣal-as i usaru-nni n tmeddurt is : 
"- Tiyita taneggarut n Buxuc, ɣas ukiɣ-as, s tidet tugar-itt tin d 
yekkan s ɣur watmaten-iw. Tiyita n Hiemsal, Aderbal, Masiwen 
akk d Gawda sfeclent-iyi. Terna-d tin n Bumelxir d timsislit. 
Anda  ilaq  tagmat  ad  tili  d  tagejdit  uɣur  ara  isenned  win 
yemdeôkalen, taggara yir tagmat terna-d aɣilif. 
Akka si zik, seg wass-mi tebda ddunit, tamurt-nneɣ ur as-tufa 
ixef-is. Si zik n zik, di yal tallit nekni neôwa akessar d usawen 
akken ad nesbedd tilisa n tmurt-nneɣ. Nezga-d ger sin icenga. 
Yiwet tama d Rruman, yiwet tama d Carthage i yegren tuccar- 
is di tmurt-nneɣ acḥal iseggasen aya. 
I sin yid-sen skecmen-aɣ di tlufa yellan gar-asen. Tikkelt d wa, 
tikkelt  d  win.  ṭṭṛad  46  ameqqran  amezwaru  d-yellan  gar-asen  
acḥal iseggasen aya, yekker ɣef tegzirt n Sisilya-Ass-mi tefra 
gar-asen,  Rruman  iḥella-d  Sisilya,  yerna-d  tigzirin  nniḍen, 
Sarda akk d Kursa.  
Carthage ur yella d tamurt s tidet. Carhage yusa-d am timmist 
deg weksum n Tamazɣa. Di tazwara-s d tiɣremt bnan Yefniqen

Carthage  yeṭṭef    tamurt  n  Tmazɣa  s  ufus  d  tidi  n  tarwa  n 
Tmazɣa. Neɣɣ iman-nneɣ s ifassen-nneɣ ! 
Di  ṭṭṛad  wis  sin  i  ɣer  yekker  jedd-i  Masensen,  yefka  tayet  i 
Rruman, dduklen ɣef uqerruy n Carthage. 
Di tedyant-nni i d iban wudem n tidet n Tmazɣa : tamurt tebḍa 
ur  teddukel.  Di  yiwet  tama  d  Tamazɣa  (Numidya)  n  ugellid

Sifaks. 
Lemmer  dduklen  igelliden,  myefken  tayet,  yili  Carthage  ad 
yenger. Lemmer dduklen, Rruman  ad  yerr  aḍar,  ad  ikukru  ad 
d-yessekcem iman-is di tmurt-nneɣ. 
Akka i tella. Di ṭṭṛad wis sin, Masensen yedda d Rruman, Sifaks 
yedda  d  Carthage.  Tama  tekka  di  tayeḍ.  Masensen  yekcem 
tiɣremt n Sirta, Sifaks icudd di snasel.

nni  yellan  ger  Tmazɣa/Muretanya  akk  d  Tmazɣa/Numidya.

tismin akk d tɣennant.

ass-a.  Beḍḍu  ger  Masensen  d  Sifaks  imir  yecba  beḍḍu  yellan

neɣ  amedyaz  ameqqran,  i  zewwiren  akken  ad  sen-yelli 
tiwwura n tmurt n medden i ran ad kecmen.

Ass-a, Rruman ibeddel. Ur yefka azal i bab igenwan, ur yessin 
abrid  n  telwit.  Anda  i  ten-tessaweḍ  tezmert-nsen,  yiɣil-nsen,  i

wakal, n wawal, n tikli, nitni ur tt-ssinen. Tga-yasen am tlafsa-
nni ur nessin tawat. 
Yella  deg  wawal  di  tmurt-nneɣ :  si  zik  n  zik,  talast  tella  ger 
wayen  yellan  d  wayen  ur  nella.  Tilisa  gan-tent  yemdanen 
akken  ad  beddent,  ad  ilint  gar-asen.  I  yal  talast  tella  tseɣlit-is. 
Tiseɣlit-nni  tella  kan  i  wallaɣ,  ur  tella  i  tezmert  ;  tella  kan 
akken  ad  yetkaki  wemdan  ansi  i  as-d-tegzem.  Dɣa,  ula  d 
izmawen  d  wuccayen  di  teẓgi  teggen  tilisa.  Yal  wa  deg 
wemḍiq-is.  Ɣas  imdanen  ur  llan  d  uccanen  neɣ  d  izmawen,  si 
talast  ɣer  da  inek,  si  talast  akin  i  kečč.  Yal  yiwen  d  amur  n 
weɣbel-is.  Amkan  deg  ur  llant  tlisa,  d  nger  kan  i  ɣur-s  d-
iteddun. 
Ugur, mačči s ɣur Rruman kan i d-yusa.  Di tidet, tella deg-neɣ 
si zik n zik. Yella wayen yelhan, yella wayen n dir. Akka !

Di Numance51, di tmurt n Spanya, i d-sneɣ tamuɣli n Rruman, 
amek ẓeôôen tamurt-nsen, amek ẓeôôen timura n medden. Lliɣ

nni n  umennuɣ di Numance mgal agellid Viriathe. 
Di  tlemmast  n  at  tmurt  i  tzemreḍ  ad  tissineḍ  at  tmurt-nni.  Di 
tlemmast  n  ṭṭṛad  i  tzemreḍ  a  tissineḍ  ugar  imdanen.  Di 
tlemmast n herwel, akken yella wemdan ara as-d-yefk udem-is, 
udem-nni  n  tidet.  Ur  yella  wurar,  ur  llant  tkerkas  ara  igen 
tagut i tidet. Di ḍḍiq, yal yiwen akken yella wudem-is i yella s 
timmad-is. Izem ad iban, awtul ur yezmir ad yentel.

zdat wallen-is ugur ameqqran : Rruman. 
Yefhem  tazzla  n  Rruman  ɣur-s  akken  ad  sen-yefk  tayet  ad 
sseɣlin Carthage, mačči i lfayda n Tmazɣa neɣ i lfayda-as netta. 
Tikli n tḥila n  Rruman i lfayda-nsen nitni : ad kksen acengu i 
yugaden  ad  yimɣur  ugar,  agemmaḍ  i  yilel  Agrakal.  Syin,  mi 
fran  tin  n  Carthage,  ad  d  zzin  i  tmura  d  ifergen  Ilel  Agrakal. 
Talast  n  Rruman  tella  kan  ansi  i  ten-id-terra  tezmert-nsen.  
Nekni  nezga  d  agemmaḍ  i  waman,    nbedd-asen  am  lɣerḍ  i 
tyita. 
Akken ad iqabel Ruma ass-mi ara d-yas wass deg ara tefru tin n 
Carthage, Masensen yeqsed ad yezwir seg tid n wexxam.  Ilaq-
as  ad  yesdukel  tamurt-is  talast  ɣer  talast.    Aɣilif  ameqqran, 
tamurt  tebḍa,  iɣisan  llan :  sya  d  tiḥdert  n  Carthage,  syin  d 
Sifaks,  tama  wadda  n  tiniri53  d  aɣeẓẓu  yal  ass.  Ur  yella 
uqerruy, ur tella telwit. 
Di tama nniḍen,  Masensen yewwet ad yessemẓi ticcerka netta 
d Ruma am akken i yessemɣer ticcerka netta d tmura nniḍen, 
yecban  Athena,  akk  d  tmurt  n  Nnil,  tamurt  n  Ferâun.  Amur 
ameqqran d azenzi n yirden d temẓin54 teddun deg yibabuôen 
ɣer Athena  neɣ akin. Di Sirta simmal llan ugar n yemdanen n 
53 Tiniri (tiniriwin) = Ṣṣeḥṛa. 
54 Di -200, Masensen yunez 200000 teqlalin (boisseaux) n yirden akk de 200000 t. 
n  temẓin  i  lâesker  n  Rruman ;  di  -198,    20000  t.  n  yirden  i  Athena ;  di  -191, 
300000  t.  n  yidren  d  250000  t.  n  temẓin  i  Ruma  akk  d  500000  t.  n  yirden  d 
300000 t.  n  temẓin  i Athena. Di  -171,  yefka  i  lâesker  n Macedoine,  1000000  t.  n 
yirden,  yerna-asen  11600  iqenṭaṛen  i  tmurt  n  Deliens.  (S-ɣur    Mouloud  GAID,

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
Athena ; deg-sen wid yetjaôen akk d wid yesselmaden tussna n 
Hellena-Di  tallit-nni  yeffeɣ  yisem  n  Tmazɣa  ugar.  Di  tmura  teddun 
yedrimen n Tmazɣa. Deg wurar ameqqran n Athena56, yezger 
baba,  Mastanabal,  yella  di  temsizzelt  igemren  deg  wennar  n 
Athena. D netta i d yeffɣen d amezwaru. 
Tikli n Masensen tedda ad tefk iẓuran i tmurt, ad teẓẓu tigejda i 
tlisa, ad tesnerni tamussni. 
Taggara, yemmut Masensen ur yessaweḍ s anda yessarem. 
D  abrid  agi  n  Masensen    i  wwteɣ  ad  t-id-berzeɣ,  ad  as-zwiɣ 
taɣebbaôt-nni n iseggasen.  Ɣas yeḍres, tuli-t tissist, abrid yella. 
Ur yezmir yiwen ad yeffer iṭij s uɣerbal. 
Abrid n jedd-i Masensen ẓriɣ d win n tidet. Greɣ aḍar-iw deg-s. 
Taggara, akken teffeɣ teffeɣ. 
Tagelda  n  Makawsen,  tebda  mi  lliɣ  di  tattalt,  deg  yirebbi  n 
yemma.    Mi  yemmut  jedd-i,  Makawsen  ibedd  d  agellid.  Ger 
watmaten-is,  baba  Mastanabal  akk  d  Gulusen  yal  yiwen 
taâkemt  yeṭṭef  deg  wegraw.  Ur  d  zin  sin  iseggasen,  am  baba-
nni am Gulusen-nni, mmuten i sin. Yegra-d Makawsen. 
Deg yimenɣi ameqqran wis 3 gar Carthage d Rruman, yekker 
Makawsen,  deg  webrid  n  Masensen,  yennuɣ  ɣer  tama  n 
Rruman.  D  win  i  d  imenɣi  aneggaru  i  d  yeglan  s  uhuddu  n 
Carthage.  D  ahuddu-nni  i  yes-s  yeẓẓa  tuẓẓal-is  Rruman  deg 
wakal n Carthage, yerra-t d ayla-s. D win i d asurif amezwaru 
unekcum n Rruman ɣer Tmazɣa. Makawsen yessusem i twaɣit-
nni.  Ur  d  yekkir  ad  iqabel  Rruman.  Yeooa-ten  fkan  imɣi  deg 
wakal-nneɣ. 
D  timmist-nni  deg  yidisan-nneɣ,  «akal  n  Rruman  »57,  i  uɣur 
tedduɣ ad t-kkseɣ. 
Ass-a  aqlaɣ  nettwarez.  Ma  nedder  ur  nemmut, 
tameqqrant ad as-neg ass-is. 
Aẓru n tesraft yettarew-d aman, irennu  tesmeḍ i tegres.  
Yugurten yuki i yiɣsan-is  simmal cerrwen tesmeḍ-nni. Akken  
tiwizi

iga  ur  as-yufa  talwit.  Yekker,  yezwi  iman-is,  yezzi  i  tesraft, 
yerna yezzi akken ad yeḥmu, yedda akka d wakka am yizem-
nni yettwarzen. Feclen yiḍaôôen-is, yeqqim. Tesmeḍ-nni tezdeɣ-
it, tegguma ad teffeɣ seg-s. 
Yeqqumec di teɣmert, isenned ɣer sin yeẓra akken ad yessenɣes 
tesmeḍ  i  weksum-is.  Tikwal,  yif  teqreḥ  tesmeḍ.  Udmawen  n 
wid  akk  yessen,  wid  iḥemmel,  wid  ur  iḥemmel,  tezzin  zdat 
wallen-is.  Tezzin  zun  llan  gar  igenni  akk  tmurt,  di  tafat  n 
tafukt tamellalt. Nitni ur zmiren ad as-ssiwlen, netta ur yezmir 
ad sen-yessiwel. Llan wid uɣur yeẓẓel iɣil-is am zun ad ten-id-
yeṭṭef. I d-yemmuger ufus-is ala ilem n tesraft. Nitni ur d-giren 
afus-nsen,  ur  as-d-zzin  udem-nsen.  Tuɣal-as  tmuɣli-nni  d 
anezgum.  Yedduqes,  yekker,  yezwi  iman-is,  yuɣal  s  awal-nni 
netta d yixef-is : 
- « Nuɣal i targit nekni nekni !  A wer nederwec ! 
Ad  kkreɣ,  ad  beddeɣ.  Amdan  ilul-d,  turew-it-id  yemma-s  s 
yibeddi,  fell-as  ad  yekker,  ad  ibedd,  ad  yazzel.    Skud  tetteddu 
tefkert n wul, yella usirem ɣer zdat.  Ma nedder, tamurt ad as 
neqqim.  Nnan  at  zik   « akken  triḍ  ɣezzifeḍ  a  yiḍ,  taggara  ad 
yali wass ». 
Di  tmuɣli  n  tudert-nneɣ  nekni,  nesdukel  tudert  n  wid  yezrin, 
am zun yid-neɣ i llan, nerna tudert-nneɣ nekni akk d tudert n 
wid  d-iteddun  ɣer  zdat.  Di  yal  ass  ɣur-neɣ,  win  ibennun  ad 
yebnu, wid iteddun ɣer zdat, i warraw n warraw-is, ɣas netta 
di ḍḍiq i yella ; win  ileqqmen iteẓẓun, ad yeẓẓu isekla ara ččen 
wid  ara  d  yefôuôxen  ɣer  zdat,  ɣas  netta  ad  yezgel  tiram. 
Amedyaz,  win  yesefruyen  awal,  di  yal  tamurt,  awal-is  iteddu 
akin  i  wussan,  akin  i  yiseggasen  ɣer  zdat,  akken  awal-nni  ad 
yili d taftilt i webrid di tagut n tmeddurt.  Ma d aḍar yettôuẓu 
asalu,  yezmer  ad  yefcel  neɣ  ad  yeâyu ;  awal  yeffal  akin  i  tizi, 
iteddu  irennu  tirkelt  i  tmussni.  Awal  ur  yezmir  yiwen  ad  t-
yeqqen, ur yezmir yiwen ad t-yekkes ma yuɣ timura, yeffeɣ am 
waḍu, yuɣ idurar d izuɣar. 
Awal-nni n tlelli, nekk ufiɣ-t deg wallen n yelmeẓyen-nneɣ, di 
yal tiɣremt i kecmeɣ di Tmazɣa, di yal taddart i ɣer unfeɣ. 
Yiwen ur yezmir ad yekkes, ad yessenger awal-nni n tlelli. 
Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 
Rruman ɣillen fran tadyant n Tmazɣa mi d-skecmen Yugurten 
deg tesraft-a n Tullianum.  Nekk ad sen-iniɣ, ur fran tigert. Ur 
yella  yiwen  Yugurten  kan  i  sen-d-yusan  d  asennan  deg 
weksum-nsen  i  Rruman.  Azekka,  yal  tiɣmert,  yal  tiɣilt,  yal 
azaɣar, yal tawrirt ad afen Yugurten ibedd-d zdat-nsen.  
Di  tikli-nni  n  Ruma,  mi  ẓriɣ  Marius  iteddu  ɣef  igemren 
imellalen,  s  ubeônus  azeggaɣ  ɣef  tuyat,  zdat-i  di  tlemmast  n 
Ruma, ẓriɣ-t am win ibedden akken ad yexbec igenni. Taẓallit- 
is ur tessirid ammus  ameqqran, ammus ugertil58, ammus n yir 
iɣil, n yir tazmert. 
Ɣurneɣ, tissas rennun i win yellan deg webrid n tissas. Ur llant 
tissas i win izegren ilel, yerẓa tilisa n tmurt n medden, yekcem 
tamurt-nsen s uqeẓẓul. 
Mi iyi-d-yeskecmen Iôumaniyen seg yimi n tesraft n 3 terdas di 
tehri, nitni ɣillen d anṭal i neṭlen Yugurten. Nwan kksen aɣilif-
nsen, wwḍen anda ssarmen. 
Nekk  ɣur-i,  anṭar-nni  i  neṭreɣ  seg  yimi  n  tesraft  ɣef  yeẓra 
isemmaḍen, d talalit tis snat.  Am lufan-nni d-ilulen si tâebbuḍt 
n yemma-s s ibeddi, yezwer-d tiwuɣa. Nekk, awal-iw ooiɣ-t-in 
ɣer deffir i warraw n tmurt-nneɣ. Awal-iw yeffeɣ, yuɣ timura, 
yezger akin i tɣaltin, ur yezmir yiwen ad t-yarez. 
Azekka, aseggas, neɣ iseggasen d iseggasen ɣer zdat, ɣas awal- 
iw  yezmer  ad  yeffer,  ad  yenṭel  tallit  neɣ  ad  tdel  tagut  tallit, 
taggara  ad  yaweḍ  wass  deg  ara  d-yefrari  i  tafat  n  tefsut,  ad 
yeddu, ad yennerni… 
58 Anhis n Tmazɣa : « Ammus ugertil : ur yetsirid ur yiṣeffeḍ ! ». 
Tallit taneggarut 
Yugurten yemmut, deffir 6 wussan n laẓ d usemmiḍ. 
Ssuffɣen-t-id  si  tesraft-nni  n  Tullianum,  wwin-t  akin,    yečča- 
wasif n Tiber, asif-nni yekkan di tlemmast n Rruman. 
Sin warraw n Yugurten i yellan ttwarzen yid-s, ur yeẓra yiwen 
anda i d-gran.  Ur nessin ismawen-nsen, ur iban webrid uɣen 
asmi  tefra  tikli-nni  n  Ruma.  Yeɣba  yisem-nsen  si  tmurt  n 
Rruman. 
Yugurten  yemmut.  Ugur  ameqqran  deg  webrid-nsen,  nwan 
yekkes-asen i Rruman. Ufan abrid di tegnit, ẓẓan tuẓẓal-nsen di 
Tmazɣa.  Deffir  Yugurten,  snulfan-d  win  sbedden  d  agellid   i 
Tmazɣa : Gawda, gma-s n Yugurten s baba-s.  Rran-t d agellid 
am lexyal- nni n tebḥirt akken ad kerzen yes-s. 
Nnan Gawda d abehlul kan, ur yessin,  ur yewzin, ur ixebbec 
ur iɣeẓ. Tamurt n Tmazɣa gezmen-tt, gezren-tt, gan-as iɣisan di 
tlemmast.  Amur  yefka-t  Rruman  i  ugellid  Buxuc,  rran-as  lxiô 
ilmend n tixubta-s, yezzenz idammen-is. 
Amur wis sin rnan-t nitni akken ad smeɣren tamurt n Carthage 
(proḍince romaine). 
Tegra-d tiḥdert n wakal, akk d tiɣremt n Sirta, yuɣal-as Gawda 
d agellid, ddaw ubeônus n Rruman ! Yuɣal d agellid ubeôwaq ! 
Taggara,  di  snat  turdas-nni  n  wakal  i  d  yegran  i  Gawda, 
yekcem  Uôumani  yal  taferka  yelhan,  yal  iger  yelhan,  yal 
tiɣremt. Tamurt tbeddel udem. 
Di tallit-nni, yeɣli-d yiḍ ɣef tmurt n Tmazɣa. Yeqqen uzaglu n 
Rruman i weɣref Amaziɣ.  Akken i teqqim ddeqs n leqrun…
